 3268   
 3269     emxFreeStruct_struct_T1(&corners2);
 3270   
 3271     //  score corners
 3272     for (i1 = 0; i1 < 3; i1++) {
 3273       dv2[i1] = 4.0 + 4.0 * (double)i1;
 3274     }
 3275   
 3276     scoreCorners(b_img, img_weight, corners3, dv2);
 3277   
 3278     //  remove low scoring corners
 3279     i1 = idx->size[0];
 3280     idx->size[0] = corners3->score->size[0];
 3281     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)idx, i1, (int)sizeof(boolean_T));
 3282     i = corners3->score->size[0];
 3283     for (i1 = 0; i1 < i; i1++) {
 3284       idx->data[i1] = (corners3->score->data[i1] < tau);
 3285     }
 3286   
 3287     nullAssignment(corners3->p, idx);
 3288     nullAssignment(corners3->v1, idx);
 3289     nullAssignment(corners3->v2, idx);
 3290     b_nullAssignment(corners3->score, idx);
 3291   
 3292     //  make v1(:,1)+v1(:,2) positive (=> comparable to c++ code)
 3293     i = corners3->v1->size[0];
 3294     i1 = idx->size[0];
 3295     idx->size[0] = i;
 3296     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)idx, i1, (int)sizeof(boolean_T));
 3297     for (i1 = 0; i1 < i; i1++) {
 3298       idx->data[i1] = (corners3->v1->data[i1] + corners3->v1->data[i1 +
 3299                        corners3->v1->size[0]] < 0.0);
 3300     }
 3301   
 3302     end = idx->size[0] - 1;
 3303     ix = 0;
 3304     for (i = 0; i <= end; i++) {
 3305       if (idx->data[i]) {
 3306         ix++;
 3307       }
 3308     }
 3309   
 3310     i1 = r1->size[0];
 3311     r1->size[0] = ix;
 3312     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)r1, i1, (int)sizeof(int));
 3313     ix = 0;
 3314     for (i = 0; i <= end; i++) {
 3315       if (idx->data[i]) {
 3316         r1->data[ix] = i + 1;
 3317         ix++;
 3318       }
 3319     }
 3320   
 3321     emxFree_boolean_T(&idx);
 3322     emxInit_real_T(&b_corners3, 2);
 3323     end = corners3->v1->size[1];
 3324     i1 = b_corners3->size[0] * b_corners3->size[1];
 3325     b_corners3->size[0] = r1->size[0];
 3326     b_corners3->size[1] = end;
 3327     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)b_corners3, i1, (int)sizeof(double));
 3328     for (i1 = 0; i1 < end; i1++) {
 3329       i = r1->size[0];
 3330       for (i2 = 0; i2 < i; i2++) {
 3331         b_corners3->data[i2 + b_corners3->size[0] * i1] = -corners3->v1->data
 3332           [(r1->data[i2] + corners3->v1->size[0] * i1) - 1];
 3333       }
 3334     }
 3335   
 3336     i = b_corners3->size[1];
 3337     for (i1 = 0; i1 < i; i1++) {
 3338       ix = b_corners3->size[0];
 3339       for (i2 = 0; i2 < ix; i2++) {
 3340         corners3->v1->data[(r1->data[i2] + corners3->v1->size[0] * i1) - 1] =
 3341           b_corners3->data[i2 + b_corners3->size[0] * i1];
 3342       }
 3343     }
 3344   
 3345     emxFree_real_T(&b_corners3);
 3346     emxFree_int32_T(&r1);
 3347     emxInit_real_T(&corners_n1, 2);
 3348   
 3349     //  make all coordinate systems right-handed (reduces matching ambiguities from 8 to 4) 
 3350     i = corners3->v1->size[0];
 3351     ix = corners3->v1->size[0] - 1;
 3352     i1 = corners_n1->size[0] * corners_n1->size[1];
 3353     corners_n1->size[0] = i;
 3354     corners_n1->size[1] = 2;
 3355     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)corners_n1, i1, (int)sizeof(double));
 3356     for (i1 = 0; i1 < i; i1++) {
 3357       corners_n1->data[i1] = corners3->v1->data[i1 + corners3->v1->size[0]];
 3358     }
 3359   
 3360     for (i1 = 0; i1 <= ix; i1++) {
 3361       corners_n1->data[i1 + corners_n1->size[0]] = -corners3->v1->data[i1];
 3362     }
 3363   
 3364     emxInit_real_T1(&x, 1);
 3365     i = corners_n1->size[0];
 3366     i1 = x->size[0];
 3367     x->size[0] = i;
 3368     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)x, i1, (int)sizeof(double));
 3369     for (i1 = 0; i1 < i; i1++) {
 3370       x->data[i1] = corners_n1->data[i1] * corners3->v2->data[i1] +
 3371         corners_n1->data[i1 + corners_n1->size[0]] * corners3->v2->data[i1 +
 3372         corners3->v2->size[0]];
 3373     }
 3374   
 3375     emxFree_real_T(&corners_n1);
 3376     emxInit_real_T1(&b_x, 1);
 3377     i1 = b_x->size[0];
 3378     b_x->size[0] = x->size[0];
 3379     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)b_x, i1, (int)sizeof(double));
 3380     i = x->size[0];
 3381     for (i1 = 0; i1 < i; i1++) {
 3382       b_x->data[i1] = x->data[i1];
 3383     }
 3384   
 3385     for (ix = 0; ix + 1 <= x->size[0]; ix++) {
 3386       if (b_x->data[ix] < 0.0) {
 3387         b_mtmp = -1.0;
 3388       } else if (b_x->data[ix] > 0.0) {
 3389         b_mtmp = 1.0;
 3390       } else if (b_x->data[ix] == 0.0) {
 3391         b_mtmp = 0.0;
 3392       } else {
 3393         b_mtmp = b_x->data[ix];
 3394       }
 3395   
 3396       b_x->data[ix] = b_mtmp;
 3397     }
 3398   
 3399     emxFree_real_T(&x);
 3400     emxInit_real_T1(&c_x, 1);
 3401     i1 = c_x->size[0];
 3402     c_x->size[0] = b_x->size[0];
 3403     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)c_x, i1, (int)sizeof(double));
 3404     i = b_x->size[0];
 3405     for (i1 = 0; i1 < i; i1++) {
 3406       c_x->data[i1] = -b_x->data[i1];
 3407     }
 3408   
 3409     emxFree_real_T(&b_x);
 3410     emxInit_real_T(&d_x, 2);
 3411     i1 = d_x->size[0] * d_x->size[1];
 3412     d_x->size[0] = c_x->size[0];
 3413     d_x->size[1] = 2;
 3414     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)d_x, i1, (int)sizeof(double));
 3415     i = c_x->size[0];
 3416     for (i1 = 0; i1 < i; i1++) {
 3417       for (i2 = 0; i2 < 2; i2++) {
 3418         d_x->data[i1 + d_x->size[0] * i2] = c_x->data[i1];
 3419       }
 3420     }
 3421   
 3422     emxFree_real_T(&c_x);
 3423     i1 = corners3->v2->size[0] * corners3->v2->size[1];
 3424     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)corners3->v2, i1, (int)sizeof(double));
 3425     i = corners3->v2->size[1];
 3426     for (i1 = 0; i1 < i; i1++) {
 3427       ix = corners3->v2->size[0];
 3428       for (i2 = 0; i2 < ix; i2++) {
 3429         corners3->v2->data[i2 + corners3->v2->size[0] * i1] *= d_x->data[i2 +
 3430           d_x->size[0] * i1];
 3431       }
 3432     }
 3433   
 3434     emxFree_real_T(&d_x);
 3435   
 3436     //  convert to 0-based index
 3437     i1 = corners3->p->size[0] * corners3->p->size[1];
 3438     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)corners3->p, i1, (int)sizeof(double));
 3439     end = corners3->p->size[0];
 3440     ix = corners3->p->size[1];
 3441     i = end * ix;
 3442     for (i1 = 0; i1 < i; i1++) {
 3443       corners3->p->data[i1]--;
 3444     }
 3445   
 3446     // disp('Find Corners OK');
 3447   }
 3448   
 3449   //
 3450   // return immediately, if there do not exist any chessboards
 3451   // Arguments    : emxArray_real_T *chessboard
 3452   //                const emxArray_real_T *corners_p
 3453   //                double border_type
 3454   // Return Type  : void
 3455   //
 3456   static void growChessboard(emxArray_real_T *chessboard, const emxArray_real_T
 3457     *corners_p, double border_type)
 3458   {
 3459     int ndbl;
 3460     int apnd;
 3461     int cdiff;
 3462     int absb;
 3463     emxArray_real_T *unused;
 3464     int i29;
 3465     emxArray_int32_T *r10;
 3466     emxArray_int32_T *b_chessboard;
 3467     emxArray_real_T *cand;
 3468     emxArray_real_T *pred;
 3469     int i30;
 3470     emxArray_real_T *idx;
 3471     emxArray_real_T *b_corners_p;
 3472     emxArray_real_T *c_corners_p;
 3473     emxArray_real_T *d_corners_p;
 3474     emxArray_boolean_T *b_idx;
 3475     emxArray_int32_T *c_idx;
 3476     boolean_T empty_non_axis_sizes;
 3477     emxArray_int32_T *d_idx;
 3478     emxArray_int32_T *e_idx;
 3479     emxArray_int32_T *f_idx;
 3480     emxArray_real_T *b_unused;
 3481     emxArray_int32_T *g_idx;
 3482     boolean_T guard2 = false;
 3483     emxArray_real_T *c_chessboard;
 3484     boolean_T guard1 = false;
 3485     if ((chessboard->size[0] == 0) || (chessboard->size[1] == 0)) {
 3486     } else {
 3487       //  extract feature locations
 3488       //  list of unused feature elements
 3489       if (corners_p->size[0] < 1) {
 3490         ndbl = 0;
 3491         apnd = 0;
 3492       } else {
 3493         ndbl = (int)floor(((double)corners_p->size[0] - 1.0) + 0.5);
 3494         apnd = ndbl + 1;
 3495         cdiff = (ndbl - corners_p->size[0]) + 1;
 3496         absb = corners_p->size[0];
 3497         if (fabs((double)cdiff) < 4.4408920985006262E-16 * (double)absb) {
 3498           ndbl++;
 3499           apnd = corners_p->size[0];
 3500         } else if (cdiff > 0) {
 3501           apnd = ndbl;
 3502         } else {
 3503           ndbl++;
 3504         }
 3505       }
 3506   
 3507       emxInit_real_T(&unused, 2);
 3508       i29 = unused->size[0] * unused->size[1];
 3509       unused->size[0] = 1;
 3510       unused->size[1] = ndbl;
 3511       emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)unused, i29, (int)sizeof(double));
 3512       if (ndbl > 0) {
 3513         unused->data[0] = 1.0;
 3514         if (ndbl > 1) {
 3515           unused->data[ndbl - 1] = apnd;
 3516           cdiff = (ndbl - 1) / 2;
 3517           for (absb = 1; absb < cdiff; absb++) {
 3518             unused->data[absb] = 1.0 + (double)absb;
 3519             unused->data[(ndbl - absb) - 1] = apnd - absb;
 3520           }
 3521   
 3522           if (cdiff << 1 == ndbl - 1) {
 3523             unused->data[cdiff] = (1.0 + (double)apnd) / 2.0;
 3524           } else {
 3525             unused->data[cdiff] = 1.0 + (double)cdiff;
 3526             unused->data[cdiff + 1] = apnd - cdiff;
 3527           }
 3528         }
 3529       }
 3530   
 3531       emxInit_int32_T(&r10, 1);
 3532       ndbl = chessboard->size[0] * chessboard->size[1] - 1;
 3533       cdiff = 0;
 3534       for (absb = 0; absb <= ndbl; absb++) {
 3535         if (chessboard->data[absb] != 0.0) {
 3536           cdiff++;
 3537         }
 3538       }
 3539   
 3540       i29 = r10->size[0];
 3541       r10->size[0] = cdiff;
 3542       emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)r10, i29, (int)sizeof(int));
 3543       cdiff = 0;
 3544       for (absb = 0; absb <= ndbl; absb++) {
 3545         if (chessboard->data[absb] != 0.0) {
 3546           r10->data[cdiff] = absb + 1;
 3547           cdiff++;
 3548         }
 3549       }
 3550   
 3551       emxInit_int32_T(&b_chessboard, 1);
 3552       i29 = b_chessboard->size[0];
 3553       b_chessboard->size[0] = r10->size[0];
 3554       emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)b_chessboard, i29, (int)sizeof(int));
 3555       apnd = r10->size[0];
 3556       for (i29 = 0; i29 < apnd; i29++) {
 3557         b_chessboard->data[i29] = (int)chessboard->data[r10->data[i29] - 1];
 3558       }
 3559   
 3560       emxFree_int32_T(&r10);
 3561       emxInit_real_T(&cand, 2);
 3562       c_nullAssignment(unused, b_chessboard);
 3563   
 3564       //  candidates from unused corners
 3565       apnd = corners_p->size[1];
 3566       i29 = cand->size[0] * cand->size[1];
 3567       cand->size[0] = unused->size[1];
 3568       cand->size[1] = apnd;
 3569       emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)cand, i29, (int)sizeof(double));
 3570       emxFree_int32_T(&b_chessboard);
 3571       for (i29 = 0; i29 < apnd; i29++) {
 3572         absb = unused->size[1];
 3573         for (i30 = 0; i30 < absb; i30++) {
 3574           cand->data[i30 + cand->size[0] * i29] = corners_p->data[((int)
 3575             unused->data[unused->size[0] * i30] + corners_p->size[0] * i29) - 1];
 3576         }
 3577       }
 3578   
 3579       //  switch border type 1..4
 3580       emxInit_real_T(&pred, 2);
 3581       emxInit_real_T(&idx, 2);
 3582       switch ((int)border_type) {
 3583        case 1:
 3584         emxInit_real_T(&b_corners_p, 2);
 3585         apnd = chessboard->size[0];
 3586         cdiff = chessboard->size[1];
 3587         absb = corners_p->size[1];
 3588         i29 = b_corners_p->size[0] * b_corners_p->size[1];
 3589         b_corners_p->size[0] = apnd;
 3590         b_corners_p->size[1] = absb;
 3591         emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)b_corners_p, i29, (int)sizeof(double));
 3592         for (i29 = 0; i29 < absb; i29++) {
 3593           for (i30 = 0; i30 < apnd; i30++) {
 3594             b_corners_p->data[i30 + b_corners_p->size[0] * i29] = corners_p->data
 3595               [((int)chessboard->data[i30 + chessboard->size[0] * (cdiff - 3)] +
 3596                 corners_p->size[0] * i29) - 1];
 3597           }
 3598         }
 3599   
 3600         emxInit_real_T(&c_corners_p, 2);
 3601         apnd = chessboard->size[0];
 3602         cdiff = chessboard->size[1];
 3603         absb = corners_p->size[1];
 3604         i29 = c_corners_p->size[0] * c_corners_p->size[1];
 3605         c_corners_p->size[0] = apnd;
 3606         c_corners_p->size[1] = absb;
 3607         emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)c_corners_p, i29, (int)sizeof(double));
 3608         for (i29 = 0; i29 < absb; i29++) {
 3609           for (i30 = 0; i30 < apnd; i30++) {
 3610             c_corners_p->data[i30 + c_corners_p->size[0] * i29] = corners_p->data
 3611               [((int)chessboard->data[i30 + chessboard->size[0] * (cdiff - 2)] +
 3612                 corners_p->size[0] * i29) - 1];
 3613           }
 3614         }
 3615   
 3616         emxInit_real_T(&d_corners_p, 2);
 3617         apnd = chessboard->size[0];
 3618         cdiff = chessboard->size[1];
 3619         absb = corners_p->size[1];
 3620         i29 = d_corners_p->size[0] * d_corners_p->size[1];
 3621         d_corners_p->size[0] = apnd;
 3622         d_corners_p->size[1] = absb;
 3623         emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)d_corners_p, i29, (int)sizeof(double));
 3624         for (i29 = 0; i29 < absb; i29++) {
 3625           for (i30 = 0; i30 < apnd; i30++) {
 3626             d_corners_p->data[i30 + d_corners_p->size[0] * i29] = corners_p->data
 3627               [((int)chessboard->data[i30 + chessboard->size[0] * (cdiff - 1)] +
 3628                 corners_p->size[0] * i29) - 1];
 3629           }
 3630         }
 3631   
 3632         emxInit_boolean_T1(&b_idx, 2);
 3633         predictCorners(b_corners_p, c_corners_p, d_corners_p, pred);
 3634         assignClosestCorners(cand, pred, idx);
 3635         i29 = b_idx->size[0] * b_idx->size[1];
 3636         b_idx->size[0] = 1;
 3637         b_idx->size[1] = idx->size[1];
 3638         emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)b_idx, i29, (int)sizeof(boolean_T));
 3639         apnd = idx->size[0] * idx->size[1];
 3640         emxFree_real_T(&d_corners_p);
 3641         emxFree_real_T(&c_corners_p);
 3642         emxFree_real_T(&b_corners_p);
 3643         for (i29 = 0; i29 < apnd; i29++) {
 3644           b_idx->data[i29] = (idx->data[i29] != 0.0);
 3645         }
 3646   
 3647         if (all(b_idx)) {
 3648           emxInit_int32_T(&c_idx, 1);
 3649           emxInit_int32_T(&d_idx, 1);
 3650           emxInit_int32_T(&e_idx, 1);
 3651           emxInit_int32_T(&f_idx, 1);
 3652           if (!((chessboard->size[0] == 0) || (chessboard->size[1] == 0))) {
 3653             cdiff = chessboard->size[0];
 3654           } else {
 3655             i29 = c_idx->size[0];
 3656             c_idx->size[0] = idx->size[1];
 3657             emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)c_idx, i29, (int)sizeof(int));
 3658             apnd = idx->size[1];
 3659             for (i29 = 0; i29 < apnd; i29++) {
 3660               c_idx->data[i29] = (int)idx->data[idx->size[0] * i29];
 3661             }
 3662   
 3663             if (!(c_idx->size[0] == 0)) {
 3664               i29 = f_idx->size[0];
 3665               f_idx->size[0] = idx->size[1];
 3666               emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)f_idx, i29, (int)sizeof(int));
 3667               apnd = idx->size[1];
 3668               for (i29 = 0; i29 < apnd; i29++) {
 3669                 f_idx->data[i29] = (int)idx->data[idx->size[0] * i29];
 3670               }
 3671   
 3672               cdiff = f_idx->size[0];
 3673             } else {
 3674               cdiff = chessboard->size[0];
 3675               if (cdiff >= 0) {
 3676               } else {
 3677                 cdiff = 0;
 3678               }
 3679   
 3680               i29 = d_idx->size[0];
 3681               d_idx->size[0] = idx->size[1];
 3682               emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)d_idx, i29, (int)sizeof(int));
 3683               apnd = idx->size[1];
 3684               for (i29 = 0; i29 < apnd; i29++) {
 3685                 d_idx->data[i29] = (int)idx->data[idx->size[0] * i29];
 3686               }
 3687   
 3688               if (d_idx->size[0] > cdiff) {
 3689                 i29 = e_idx->size[0];
 3690                 e_idx->size[0] = idx->size[1];
 3691                 emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)e_idx, i29, (int)sizeof(int));
 3692                 apnd = idx->size[1];
 3693                 for (i29 = 0; i29 < apnd; i29++) {
 3694                   e_idx->data[i29] = (int)idx->data[idx->size[0] * i29];
 3695                 }
 3696   
 3697                 cdiff = e_idx->size[0];
 3698               }
 3699             }
 3700           }
 3701   
 3702           emxFree_int32_T(&f_idx);
 3703           emxFree_int32_T(&e_idx);
 3704           emxFree_int32_T(&d_idx);
 3705           emxFree_int32_T(&c_idx);
 3706           empty_non_axis_sizes = (cdiff == 0);
 3707           if (empty_non_axis_sizes || (!((chessboard->size[0] == 0) ||
 3708                 (chessboard->size[1] == 0)))) {
 3709             absb = chessboard->size[1];
 3710           } else {
 3711             absb = 0;
 3712           }
 3713   
 3714           emxInit_int32_T(&g_idx, 1);
 3715           guard2 = false;
 3716           if (empty_non_axis_sizes) {
 3717             guard2 = true;
 3718           } else {
 3719             i29 = g_idx->size[0];
 3720             g_idx->size[0] = idx->size[1];
 3721             emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)g_idx, i29, (int)sizeof(int));
 3722             apnd = idx->size[1];
 3723             for (i29 = 0; i29 < apnd; i29++) {
 3724               g_idx->data[i29] = (int)idx->data[idx->size[0] * i29];
 3725             }
 3726   
 3727             if (!(g_idx->size[0] == 0)) {
 3728               guard2 = true;
 3729             } else {
 3730               ndbl = 0;
 3731             }
 3732           }
 3733   
 3734           if (guard2) {
 3735             ndbl = 1;
 3736           }
 3737   
 3738           emxFree_int32_T(&g_idx);
 3739           emxInit_real_T1(&b_unused, 1);
 3740           i29 = b_unused->size[0];
 3741           b_unused->size[0] = idx->size[1];
 3742           emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)b_unused, i29, (int)sizeof(double));
 3743           apnd = idx->size[1];
 3744           for (i29 = 0; i29 < apnd; i29++) {
 3745             b_unused->data[i29] = unused->data[(int)idx->data[idx->size[0] * i29]
 3746               - 1];
 3747           }
 3748   
 3749           emxInit_real_T(&c_chessboard, 2);
 3750           i29 = c_chessboard->size[0] * c_chessboard->size[1];
 3751           c_chessboard->size[0] = cdiff;
 3752           c_chessboard->size[1] = absb + ndbl;
 3753           emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)c_chessboard, i29, (int)sizeof
