 4222             absb = 0;
 4223           }
 4224   
 4225           if (empty_non_axis_sizes || (!((chessboard->size[0] == 0) ||
 4226                 (chessboard->size[1] == 0)))) {
 4227             ndbl = chessboard->size[0];
 4228           } else {
 4229             ndbl = 0;
 4230           }
 4231   
 4232           emxInit_real_T(&b_unused, 2);
 4233           i29 = b_unused->size[0] * b_unused->size[1];
 4234           b_unused->size[0] = 1;
 4235           b_unused->size[1] = idx->size[1];
 4236           emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)b_unused, i29, (int)sizeof(double));
 4237           apnd = idx->size[1];
 4238           for (i29 = 0; i29 < apnd; i29++) {
 4239             b_unused->data[b_unused->size[0] * i29] = unused->data[(int)idx->
 4240               data[idx->size[0] * i29] - 1];
 4241           }
 4242   
 4243           emxInit_real_T(&c_chessboard, 2);
 4244           i29 = c_chessboard->size[0] * c_chessboard->size[1];
 4245           c_chessboard->size[0] = absb + ndbl;
 4246           c_chessboard->size[1] = cdiff;
 4247           emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)c_chessboard, i29, (int)sizeof
 4248                             (double));
 4249           for (i29 = 0; i29 < cdiff; i29++) {
 4250             for (i30 = 0; i30 < absb; i30++) {
 4251               c_chessboard->data[i30 + c_chessboard->size[0] * i29] =
 4252                 b_unused->data[i30 + absb * i29];
 4253             }
 4254           }
 4255   
 4256           emxFree_real_T(&b_unused);
 4257           for (i29 = 0; i29 < cdiff; i29++) {
 4258             for (i30 = 0; i30 < ndbl; i30++) {
 4259               c_chessboard->data[(i30 + absb) + c_chessboard->size[0] * i29] =
 4260                 chessboard->data[i30 + ndbl * i29];
 4261             }
 4262           }
 4263   
 4264           i29 = chessboard->size[0] * chessboard->size[1];
 4265           chessboard->size[0] = c_chessboard->size[0];
 4266           chessboard->size[1] = c_chessboard->size[1];
 4267           emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)chessboard, i29, (int)sizeof
 4268                             (double));
 4269           apnd = c_chessboard->size[1];
 4270           for (i29 = 0; i29 < apnd; i29++) {
 4271             absb = c_chessboard->size[0];
 4272             for (i30 = 0; i30 < absb; i30++) {
 4273               chessboard->data[i30 + chessboard->size[0] * i29] =
 4274                 c_chessboard->data[i30 + c_chessboard->size[0] * i29];
 4275             }
 4276           }
 4277   
 4278           emxFree_real_T(&c_chessboard);
 4279         }
 4280   
 4281         emxFree_boolean_T(&b_idx);
 4282         break;
 4283       }
 4284   
 4285       emxFree_real_T(&idx);
 4286       emxFree_real_T(&pred);
 4287       emxFree_real_T(&cand);
 4288       emxFree_real_T(&unused);
 4289     }
 4290   }
 4291   
 4292   //
 4293   // return if not enough corners
 4294   // Arguments    : const emxArray_real_T *corners_p
 4295   //                const emxArray_real_T *corners_v1
 4296   //                const emxArray_real_T *corners_v2
 4297   //                double idx
 4298   //                emxArray_real_T *chessboard
 4299   // Return Type  : void
 4300   //
 4301   static void initChessboard(const emxArray_real_T *corners_p, const
 4302     emxArray_real_T *corners_v1, const emxArray_real_T *corners_v2, double idx,
 4303     emxArray_real_T *chessboard)
 4304   {
 4305     int k;
 4306     emxArray_real_T *v1;
 4307     int ix;
 4308     emxArray_real_T *v2;
 4309     emxArray_real_T *b_chessboard;
 4310     emxArray_real_T *b_v1;
 4311     double dist1[2];
 4312     emxArray_real_T *c_chessboard;
 4313     emxArray_real_T *d_chessboard;
 4314     emxArray_real_T *b_v2;
 4315     double dist2[6];
 4316     emxArray_real_T *e_chessboard;
 4317     emxArray_real_T *c_v2;
 4318     emxArray_real_T *f_chessboard;
 4319     emxArray_real_T *g_chessboard;
 4320     emxArray_real_T *d_v2;
 4321     emxArray_real_T *h_chessboard;
 4322     emxArray_real_T *i_chessboard;
 4323     boolean_T x[2];
 4324     boolean_T y;
 4325     boolean_T exitg2;
 4326     boolean_T guard1 = false;
 4327     boolean_T b_x[6];
 4328     boolean_T exitg1;
 4329     double xbar;
 4330     double r;
 4331     double b_y;
 4332     if (corners_p->size[0] < 9) {
 4333       k = chessboard->size[0] * chessboard->size[1];
 4334       chessboard->size[0] = 0;
 4335       chessboard->size[1] = 0;
 4336       emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)chessboard, k, (int)sizeof(double));
 4337     } else {
 4338       //  init chessboard hypothesis
 4339       k = chessboard->size[0] * chessboard->size[1];
 4340       chessboard->size[0] = 3;
 4341       chessboard->size[1] = 3;
 4342       emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)chessboard, k, (int)sizeof(double));
 4343       for (k = 0; k < 9; k++) {
 4344         chessboard->data[k] = 0.0;
 4345       }
 4346   
 4347       emxInit_real_T(&v1, 2);
 4348   
 4349       //  extract feature index and orientation (central element)
 4350       ix = corners_v1->size[1];
 4351       k = v1->size[0] * v1->size[1];
 4352       v1->size[0] = 1;
 4353       v1->size[1] = ix;
 4354       emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)v1, k, (int)sizeof(double));
 4355       for (k = 0; k < ix; k++) {
 4356         v1->data[v1->size[0] * k] = corners_v1->data[((int)idx + corners_v1->size
 4357           [0] * k) - 1];
 4358       }
 4359   
 4360       emxInit_real_T(&v2, 2);
 4361       ix = corners_v2->size[1];
 4362       k = v2->size[0] * v2->size[1];
 4363       v2->size[0] = 1;
 4364       v2->size[1] = ix;
 4365       emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)v2, k, (int)sizeof(double));
 4366       for (k = 0; k < ix; k++) {
 4367         v2->data[v2->size[0] * k] = corners_v2->data[((int)idx + corners_v2->size
 4368           [0] * k) - 1];
 4369       }
 4370   
 4371       emxInit_real_T(&b_chessboard, 2);
 4372       chessboard->data[1 + chessboard->size[0]] = idx;
 4373   
 4374       //  find left/right/top/bottom neighbors
 4375       k = b_chessboard->size[0] * b_chessboard->size[1];
 4376       b_chessboard->size[0] = chessboard->size[0];
 4377       b_chessboard->size[1] = chessboard->size[1];
 4378       emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)b_chessboard, k, (int)sizeof(double));
 4379       ix = chessboard->size[0] * chessboard->size[1];
 4380       for (k = 0; k < ix; k++) {
 4381         b_chessboard->data[k] = chessboard->data[k];
 4382       }
 4383   
 4384       emxInit_real_T(&b_v1, 2);
 4385       directionalNeighbor(idx, v1, b_chessboard, corners_p, &chessboard->data[1 +
 4386                           (chessboard->size[0] << 1)], &dist1[0]);
 4387       k = b_v1->size[0] * b_v1->size[1];
 4388       b_v1->size[0] = 1;
 4389       b_v1->size[1] = v1->size[1];
 4390       emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)b_v1, k, (int)sizeof(double));
 4391       ix = v1->size[0] * v1->size[1];
 4392       emxFree_real_T(&b_chessboard);
 4393       for (k = 0; k < ix; k++) {
 4394         b_v1->data[k] = -v1->data[k];
 4395       }
 4396   
 4397       emxFree_real_T(&v1);
 4398       emxInit_real_T(&c_chessboard, 2);
 4399       k = c_chessboard->size[0] * c_chessboard->size[1];
 4400       c_chessboard->size[0] = chessboard->size[0];
 4401       c_chessboard->size[1] = chessboard->size[1];
 4402       emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)c_chessboard, k, (int)sizeof(double));
 4403       ix = chessboard->size[0] * chessboard->size[1];
 4404       for (k = 0; k < ix; k++) {
 4405         c_chessboard->data[k] = chessboard->data[k];
 4406       }
 4407   
 4408       emxInit_real_T(&d_chessboard, 2);
 4409       directionalNeighbor(idx, b_v1, c_chessboard, corners_p, &chessboard->data[1],
 4410                           &dist1[1]);
 4411       k = d_chessboard->size[0] * d_chessboard->size[1];
 4412       d_chessboard->size[0] = chessboard->size[0];
 4413       d_chessboard->size[1] = chessboard->size[1];
 4414       emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)d_chessboard, k, (int)sizeof(double));
 4415       ix = chessboard->size[0] * chessboard->size[1];
 4416       emxFree_real_T(&c_chessboard);
 4417       emxFree_real_T(&b_v1);
 4418       for (k = 0; k < ix; k++) {
 4419         d_chessboard->data[k] = chessboard->data[k];
 4420       }
 4421   
 4422       emxInit_real_T(&b_v2, 2);
 4423       directionalNeighbor(idx, v2, d_chessboard, corners_p, &chessboard->data[2 +
 4424                           chessboard->size[0]], &dist2[0]);
 4425       k = b_v2->size[0] * b_v2->size[1];
 4426       b_v2->size[0] = 1;
 4427       b_v2->size[1] = v2->size[1];
 4428       emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)b_v2, k, (int)sizeof(double));
 4429       ix = v2->size[0] * v2->size[1];
 4430       emxFree_real_T(&d_chessboard);
 4431       for (k = 0; k < ix; k++) {
 4432         b_v2->data[k] = -v2->data[k];
 4433       }
 4434   
 4435       emxInit_real_T(&e_chessboard, 2);
 4436       k = e_chessboard->size[0] * e_chessboard->size[1];
 4437       e_chessboard->size[0] = chessboard->size[0];
 4438       e_chessboard->size[1] = chessboard->size[1];
 4439       emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)e_chessboard, k, (int)sizeof(double));
 4440       ix = chessboard->size[0] * chessboard->size[1];
 4441       for (k = 0; k < ix; k++) {
 4442         e_chessboard->data[k] = chessboard->data[k];
 4443       }
 4444   
 4445       emxInit_real_T(&c_v2, 2);
 4446       directionalNeighbor(idx, b_v2, e_chessboard, corners_p, &chessboard->
 4447                           data[chessboard->size[0]], &dist2[1]);
 4448   
 4449       //  find top-left/top-right/bottom-left/bottom-right neighbors
 4450       k = c_v2->size[0] * c_v2->size[1];
 4451       c_v2->size[0] = 1;
 4452       c_v2->size[1] = v2->size[1];
 4453       emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)c_v2, k, (int)sizeof(double));
 4454       ix = v2->size[0] * v2->size[1];
 4455       emxFree_real_T(&e_chessboard);
 4456       emxFree_real_T(&b_v2);
 4457       for (k = 0; k < ix; k++) {
 4458         c_v2->data[k] = -v2->data[k];
 4459       }
 4460   
 4461       emxInit_real_T(&f_chessboard, 2);
 4462       k = f_chessboard->size[0] * f_chessboard->size[1];
 4463       f_chessboard->size[0] = chessboard->size[0];
 4464       f_chessboard->size[1] = chessboard->size[1];
 4465       emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)f_chessboard, k, (int)sizeof(double));
 4466       ix = chessboard->size[0] * chessboard->size[1];
 4467       for (k = 0; k < ix; k++) {
 4468         f_chessboard->data[k] = chessboard->data[k];
 4469       }
 4470   
 4471       emxInit_real_T(&g_chessboard, 2);
 4472       directionalNeighbor(chessboard->data[1], c_v2, f_chessboard, corners_p,
 4473                           &chessboard->data[0], &dist2[2]);
 4474       k = g_chessboard->size[0] * g_chessboard->size[1];
 4475       g_chessboard->size[0] = chessboard->size[0];
 4476       g_chessboard->size[1] = chessboard->size[1];
 4477       emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)g_chessboard, k, (int)sizeof(double));
 4478       ix = chessboard->size[0] * chessboard->size[1];
 4479       emxFree_real_T(&f_chessboard);
 4480       emxFree_real_T(&c_v2);
 4481       for (k = 0; k < ix; k++) {
 4482         g_chessboard->data[k] = chessboard->data[k];
 4483       }
 4484   
 4485       emxInit_real_T(&d_v2, 2);
 4486       directionalNeighbor(chessboard->data[1], v2, g_chessboard, corners_p,
 4487                           &chessboard->data[2], &dist2[3]);
 4488       k = d_v2->size[0] * d_v2->size[1];
 4489       d_v2->size[0] = 1;
 4490       d_v2->size[1] = v2->size[1];
 4491       emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)d_v2, k, (int)sizeof(double));
 4492       ix = v2->size[0] * v2->size[1];
 4493       emxFree_real_T(&g_chessboard);
 4494       for (k = 0; k < ix; k++) {
 4495         d_v2->data[k] = -v2->data[k];
 4496       }
 4497   
 4498       emxInit_real_T(&h_chessboard, 2);
 4499       k = h_chessboard->size[0] * h_chessboard->size[1];
 4500       h_chessboard->size[0] = chessboard->size[0];
 4501       h_chessboard->size[1] = chessboard->size[1];
 4502       emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)h_chessboard, k, (int)sizeof(double));
 4503       ix = chessboard->size[0] * chessboard->size[1];
 4504       for (k = 0; k < ix; k++) {
 4505         h_chessboard->data[k] = chessboard->data[k];
 4506       }
 4507   
 4508       emxInit_real_T(&i_chessboard, 2);
 4509       directionalNeighbor(chessboard->data[1 + (chessboard->size[0] << 1)], d_v2,
 4510                           h_chessboard, corners_p, &chessboard->data
 4511                           [chessboard->size[0] << 1], &dist2[4]);
 4512       k = i_chessboard->size[0] * i_chessboard->size[1];
 4513       i_chessboard->size[0] = chessboard->size[0];
 4514       i_chessboard->size[1] = chessboard->size[1];
 4515       emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)i_chessboard, k, (int)sizeof(double));
 4516       ix = chessboard->size[0] * chessboard->size[1];
 4517       emxFree_real_T(&h_chessboard);
 4518       emxFree_real_T(&d_v2);
 4519       for (k = 0; k < ix; k++) {
 4520         i_chessboard->data[k] = chessboard->data[k];
 4521       }
 4522   
 4523       directionalNeighbor(chessboard->data[1 + (chessboard->size[0] << 1)], v2,
 4524                           i_chessboard, corners_p, &chessboard->data[2 +
 4525                           (chessboard->size[0] << 1)], &dist2[5]);
 4526   
 4527       //  initialization must be homogenously distributed
 4528       emxFree_real_T(&i_chessboard);
 4529       emxFree_real_T(&v2);
 4530       for (k = 0; k < 2; k++) {
 4531         x[k] = rtIsInf(dist1[k]);
 4532       }
 4533   
 4534       y = false;
 4535       k = 0;
 4536       exitg2 = false;
 4537       while ((!exitg2) && (k < 2)) {
 4538         if (!!x[k]) {
 4539           y = true;
 4540           exitg2 = true;
 4541         } else {
 4542           k++;
 4543         }
 4544       }
 4545   
 4546       guard1 = false;
 4547       if (y) {
 4548         guard1 = true;
 4549       } else {
 4550         for (k = 0; k < 6; k++) {
 4551           b_x[k] = rtIsInf(dist2[k]);
 4552         }
 4553   
 4554         y = false;
 4555         k = 0;
 4556         exitg1 = false;
 4557         while ((!exitg1) && (k < 6)) {
 4558           if (!!b_x[k]) {
 4559             y = true;
 4560             exitg1 = true;
 4561           } else {
 4562             k++;
 4563           }
 4564         }
 4565   
 4566         if (y) {
 4567           guard1 = true;
 4568         } else {
 4569           xbar = (dist1[0] + dist1[1]) / 2.0;
 4570           r = dist1[0] - xbar;
 4571           xbar = dist1[1] - xbar;
 4572           if (sqrt(r * r + xbar * xbar) / ((dist1[0] + dist1[1]) / 2.0) > 0.3) {
 4573             guard1 = true;
 4574           } else {
 4575             ix = 0;
 4576             xbar = dist2[0];
 4577             for (k = 0; k < 5; k++) {
 4578               ix++;
 4579               xbar += dist2[ix];
 4580             }
 4581   
 4582             xbar /= 6.0;
 4583             ix = 0;
 4584             r = dist2[0] - xbar;
 4585             b_y = r * r;
 4586             for (k = 0; k < 5; k++) {
 4587               ix++;
 4588               r = dist2[ix] - xbar;
 4589               b_y += r * r;
 4590             }
 4591   
 4592             b_y /= 5.0;
 4593             xbar = dist2[0];
 4594             for (k = 0; k < 5; k++) {
 4595               xbar += dist2[k + 1];
 4596             }
 4597   
 4598             if (sqrt(b_y) / (xbar / 6.0) > 0.3) {
 4599               guard1 = true;
 4600             }
 4601           }
 4602         }
 4603       }
 4604   
 4605       if (guard1) {
 4606         k = chessboard->size[0] * chessboard->size[1];
 4607         chessboard->size[0] = 0;
 4608         chessboard->size[1] = 0;
 4609         emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)chessboard, k, (int)sizeof(double));
 4610       }
 4611     }
 4612   }
 4613   
 4614   //
 4615   // Arguments    : const emxArray_real_T *x
 4616   // Return Type  : double
 4617   //
 4618   static double mean(const emxArray_real_T *x)
 4619   {
 4620     double y;
 4621     int k;
 4622     if (x->size[0] == 0) {
 4623       y = 0.0;
 4624     } else {
 4625       y = x->data[0];
 4626       for (k = 2; k <= x->size[0]; k++) {
 4627         y += x->data[k - 1];
 4628       }
 4629     }
 4630   
 4631     y /= (double)x->size[0];
 4632     return y;
 4633   }
 4634   
 4635   //
 4636   // Arguments    : emxArray_int32_T *idx
 4637   //                emxArray_real_T *x
 4638   //                int offset
 4639   //                int np
 4640   //                int nq
 4641   //                emxArray_int32_T *iwork
 4642   //                emxArray_real_T *xwork
 4643   // Return Type  : void
 4644   //
 4645   static void merge(emxArray_int32_T *idx, emxArray_real_T *x, int offset, int np,
 4646                     int nq, emxArray_int32_T *iwork, emxArray_real_T *xwork)
 4647   {
 4648     int n;
 4649     int qend;
 4650     int p;
 4651     int iout;
 4652     int exitg1;
 4653     if ((np == 0) || (nq == 0)) {
 4654     } else {
 4655       n = np + nq;
 4656       for (qend = 0; qend + 1 <= n; qend++) {
 4657         iwork->data[qend] = idx->data[offset + qend];
 4658         xwork->data[qend] = x->data[offset + qend];
 4659       }
 4660   
 4661       p = 0;
 4662       n = np;
 4663       qend = np + nq;
 4664       iout = offset - 1;
 4665       do {
 4666         exitg1 = 0;
 4667         iout++;
 4668         if (xwork->data[p] >= xwork->data[n]) {
 4669           idx->data[iout] = iwork->data[p];
 4670           x->data[iout] = xwork->data[p];
 4671           if (p + 1 < np) {
 4672             p++;
 4673           } else {
 4674             exitg1 = 1;
 4675           }
 4676         } else {
 4677           idx->data[iout] = iwork->data[n];
 4678           x->data[iout] = xwork->data[n];
 4679           if (n + 1 < qend) {
 4680             n++;
 4681           } else {
 4682             n = iout - p;
 4683             while (p + 1 <= np) {
 4684               idx->data[(n + p) + 1] = iwork->data[p];
 4685               x->data[(n + p) + 1] = xwork->data[p];
 4686               p++;
 4687             }
 4688   
 4689             exitg1 = 1;
 4690           }
 4691         }
 4692       } while (exitg1 == 0);
 4693     }
 4694   }
 4695   
 4696   //
 4697   // Arguments    : emxArray_int32_T *idx
 4698   //                emxArray_real_T *x
 4699   //                int offset
 4700   //                int n
 4701   //                int preSortLevel
 4702   //                emxArray_int32_T *iwork
 4703   //                emxArray_real_T *xwork
 4704   // Return Type  : void
 4705   //
 4706   static void merge_block(emxArray_int32_T *idx, emxArray_real_T *x, int offset,
 4707     int n, int preSortLevel, emxArray_int32_T *iwork, emxArray_real_T *xwork)
 4708   {
 4709     int nPairs;
 4710     int bLen;
 4711     int tailOffset;
 4712     int nTail;
 4713     nPairs = n >> preSortLevel;
 4714     bLen = 1 << preSortLevel;
 4715     while (nPairs > 1) {
 4716       if ((nPairs & 1) != 0) {
 4717         nPairs--;
 4718         tailOffset = bLen * nPairs;
 4719         nTail = n - tailOffset;
 4720         if (nTail > bLen) {
 4721           merge(idx, x, offset + tailOffset, bLen, nTail - bLen, iwork, xwork);
 4722         }
 4723       }
 4724   
 4725       tailOffset = bLen << 1;
 4726       nPairs >>= 1;
 4727       for (nTail = 1; nTail <= nPairs; nTail++) {
 4728         merge(idx, x, offset + (nTail - 1) * tailOffset, bLen, bLen, iwork, xwork);
 4729       }
 4730   
 4731       bLen = tailOffset;
 4732     }
 4733   
 4734     if (n > bLen) {
 4735       merge(idx, x, offset, bLen, n - bLen, iwork, xwork);
 4736     }
 4737   }
 4738   
 4739   //
 4740   // extract parameters
 4741   // Arguments    : const double img[921600]
 4742   //                double tau
 4743   //                emxArray_real_T *maxima
 4744   // Return Type  : void
 4745   //
 4746   static void nonMaximumSuppression(const double img[921600], double tau,
 4747     emxArray_real_T *maxima)
 4748   {
 4749     int i3;
 4750     emxArray_real_T *b_maxima;
 4751     int i;
 4752     int b_i;
 4753     int j;
 4754     int b_j;
 4755     int maxi;
 4756     int maxj;
 4757     double maxval;
 4758     int i2;
 4759     int failed;
 4760     int b_i2;
 4761     int j2;
 4762     boolean_T exitg1;
 4763     int b_j2;
 4764     int result;
 4765     boolean_T exitg2;
 4766     int i4;
 4767     int loop_ub;
 4768   
 4769     //  init maxima list
 4770     i3 = maxima->size[0] * maxima->size[1];
 4771     maxima->size[0] = 0;
 4772     maxima->size[1] = 0;
 4773     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)maxima, i3, (int)sizeof(double));
 4774   
 4775     //  non maximum suppression
 4776     emxInit_real_T(&b_maxima, 2);
 4777     for (i = 0; i < 316; i++) {
 4778       b_i = 8 + (i << 2);
 4779       for (j = 0; j < 176; j++) {
 4780         b_j = 8 + (j << 2);
 4781         maxi = b_i + 1;
 4782         maxj = b_j + 1;
 4783         maxval = img[b_j + 720 * b_i];
 4784         for (i2 = 0; i2 < 4; i2++) {
 4785           b_i2 = b_i + i2;
 4786           for (j2 = 0; j2 < 4; j2++) {
 4787             b_j2 = b_j + j2;
 4788             if (img[b_j2 + 720 * b_i2] > maxval) {
 4789               maxi = b_i2 + 1;
 4790               maxj = b_j2 + 1;
 4791               maxval = img[b_j2 + 720 * b_i2];
 4792             }
 4793           }
 4794         }
 4795   
 4796         failed = 0;
 4797         i2 = 0;
 4798         exitg1 = false;
 4799         while ((!exitg1) && (i2 <= 6)) {
 4800           b_i2 = (maxi + i2) - 3;
 4801           j2 = 0;
 4802           exitg2 = false;
 4803           while ((!exitg2) && (j2 <= 6)) {
 4804             b_j2 = (maxj + j2) - 3;
 4805             if ((img[(b_j2 + 720 * (b_i2 - 1)) - 1] > maxval) && ((b_i2 < b_i + 1)
 4806                  || (b_i2 > b_i + 4) || (b_j2 < b_j + 1) || (b_j2 > b_j + 4))) {
 4807               failed = 1;
 4808               exitg2 = true;
 4809             } else {
 4810               j2++;
 4811             }
 4812           }
 4813   
 4814           if (failed != 0) {
 4815             exitg1 = true;
 4816           } else {
 4817             i2++;
 4818           }
 4819         }
 4820   
 4821         if ((maxval >= tau) && (!(failed != 0))) {
 4822           if (!((maxima->size[0] == 0) || (maxima->size[1] == 0))) {
 4823             result = maxima->size[0];
 4824           } else {
 4825             result = 0;
 4826           }
 4827   
 4828           i3 = b_maxima->size[0] * b_maxima->size[1];
 4829           b_maxima->size[0] = result + 1;
 4830           b_maxima->size[1] = 2;
 4831           emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)b_maxima, i3, (int)sizeof(double));
 4832           for (i3 = 0; i3 < 2; i3++) {
 4833             for (i4 = 0; i4 < result; i4++) {
 4834               b_maxima->data[i4 + b_maxima->size[0] * i3] = maxima->data[i4 +
 4835                 result * i3];
 4836             }
 4837           }
 4838   
 4839           b_maxima->data[result] = maxi;
 4840           b_maxima->data[result + b_maxima->size[0]] = maxj;
 4841           i3 = maxima->size[0] * maxima->size[1];
 4842           maxima->size[0] = b_maxima->size[0];
 4843           maxima->size[1] = b_maxima->size[1];
 4844           emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)maxima, i3, (int)sizeof(double));
 4845           result = b_maxima->size[1];
 4846           for (i3 = 0; i3 < result; i3++) {
 4847             loop_ub = b_maxima->size[0];
 4848             for (i4 = 0; i4 < loop_ub; i4++) {
 4849               maxima->data[i4 + maxima->size[0] * i3] = b_maxima->data[i4 +
 4850                 b_maxima->size[0] * i3];
 4851             }
 4852           }
 4853         }
 4854       }
 4855     }
 4856   
 4857     emxFree_real_T(&b_maxima);
 4858   }
 4859   
 4860   //
 4861   // Arguments    : const double x[2]
 4862   // Return Type  : double
 4863   //
 4864   static double norm(const double x[2])
 4865   {
 4866     double y;
 4867     double scale;
 4868     int k;
 4869     double absxk;
 4870     double t;
 4871     y = 0.0;
 4872     scale = 2.2250738585072014E-308;
 4873     for (k = 0; k < 2; k++) {
 4874       absxk = fabs(x[k]);
 4875       if (absxk > scale) {
 4876         t = scale / absxk;
 4877         y = 1.0 + y * t * t;
 4878         scale = absxk;
 4879       } else {
 4880         t = absxk / scale;
 4881         y += t * t;
 4882       }
 4883     }
 4884   
 4885     return scale * sqrt(y);
 4886   }
 4887   
 4888   //
 4889   // Arguments    : emxArray_real_T *x
 4890   //                const emxArray_boolean_T *idx
 4891   // Return Type  : void
 4892   //
 4893   static void nullAssignment(emxArray_real_T *x, const emxArray_boolean_T *idx)
 4894   {
 4895     int nrowx;
 4896     int ncolx;
 4897     int nrows;
 4898     int k;
 4899     int i;
 4900     int j;
 4901     emxArray_real_T *b_x;
 4902     nrowx = x->size[0];
 4903     ncolx = x->size[1];
 4904     nrows = 0;
 4905     for (k = 1; k <= idx->size[0]; k++) {
 4906       nrows += idx->data[k - 1];
 4907     }
 4908   
 4909     nrows = x->size[0] - nrows;
 4910     i = 0;
 4911     for (k = 1; k <= nrowx; k++) {
 4912       if ((k > idx->size[0]) || (!idx->data[k - 1])) {
 4913         for (j = 0; j + 1 <= ncolx; j++) {
 4914           x->data[i + x->size[0] * j] = x->data[(k + x->size[0] * j) - 1];
 4915         }
 4916   
 4917         i++;
 4918       }
 4919     }
 4920   
 4921     if (1 > nrows) {
 4922       i = 0;
 4923     } else {
 4924       i = nrows;
 4925     }
 4926   
 4927     emxInit_real_T(&b_x, 2);
 4928     nrows = x->size[1];
 4929     j = b_x->size[0] * b_x->size[1];
 4930     b_x->size[0] = i;
 4931     b_x->size[1] = nrows;
 4932     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)b_x, j, (int)sizeof(double));
 4933     for (j = 0; j < nrows; j++) {
 4934       for (nrowx = 0; nrowx < i; nrowx++) {
 4935         b_x->data[nrowx + b_x->size[0] * j] = x->data[nrowx + x->size[0] * j];
 4936       }
 4937     }
 4938   
 4939     j = x->size[0] * x->size[1];
 4940     x->size[0] = b_x->size[0];
 4941     x->size[1] = b_x->size[1];
 4942     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)x, j, (int)sizeof(double));
 4943     i = b_x->size[1];
 4944     for (j = 0; j < i; j++) {
 4945       nrows = b_x->size[0];
 4946       for (nrowx = 0; nrowx < nrows; nrowx++) {
 4947         x->data[nrowx + x->size[0] * j] = b_x->data[nrowx + b_x->size[0] * j];
 4948       }
 4949     }
 4950   
 4951     emxFree_real_T(&b_x);
 4952   }
 4953   
 4954   //
 4955   // Arguments    : const double a[921600]
 4956   //                double y[921600]
 4957   // Return Type  : void
 4958   //
 4959   static void power(const double a[921600], double y[921600])
 4960   {
 4961     int k;
 4962     for (k = 0; k < 921600; k++) {
 4963       y[k] = a[k] * a[k];
 4964     }
 4965   }
 4966   
 4967   //
 4968   // compute vectors
 4969   // Arguments    : const emxArray_real_T *p1
 4970   //                const emxArray_real_T *p2
 4971   //                const emxArray_real_T *p3
 4972   //                emxArray_real_T *pred
 4973   // Return Type  : void
 4974   //
 4975   static void predictCorners(const emxArray_real_T *p1, const emxArray_real_T *p2,
 4976     const emxArray_real_T *p3, emxArray_real_T *pred)
 4977   {
 4978     emxArray_real_T *v1;
 4979     int k;
 4980     int loop_ub;
 4981     emxArray_real_T *v2;
 4982     emxArray_real_T *b_v1;
 4983     emxArray_real_T *c_v1;
 4984     emxArray_real_T *a1;
 4985     emxArray_real_T *b_v2;
 4986     emxArray_real_T *c_v2;
 4987     emxArray_real_T *a3;
 4988     emxArray_real_T *d_v1;
 4989     emxArray_real_T *s1;
 4990     emxArray_real_T *e_v1;
 4991     emxArray_real_T *d_v2;
 4992     emxArray_real_T *b;
 4993     emxArray_real_T *e_v2;
 4994     emxArray_real_T *x;
 4995     emxArray_real_T *r7;
 4996     emxArray_real_T *r8;
 4997     emxArray_real_T *b_a1;
 4998     int i12;
 4999     int b_loop_ub;
 5000     emxInit_real_T(&v1, 2);
 5001     k = v1->size[0] * v1->size[1];
 5002     v1->size[0] = p2->size[0];
 5003     v1->size[1] = p2->size[1];
 5004     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)v1, k, (int)sizeof(double));
 5005     loop_ub = p2->size[0] * p2->size[1];
 5006     for (k = 0; k < loop_ub; k++) {
 5007       v1->data[k] = p2->data[k] - p1->data[k];
 5008     }
 5009   
 5010     emxInit_real_T(&v2, 2);
 5011     k = v2->size[0] * v2->size[1];
 5012     v2->size[0] = p3->size[0];
 5013     v2->size[1] = p3->size[1];
 5014     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)v2, k, (int)sizeof(double));
 5015     loop_ub = p3->size[0] * p3->size[1];
 5016     for (k = 0; k < loop_ub; k++) {
 5017       v2->data[k] = p3->data[k] - p2->data[k];
 5018     }
 5019   
 5020     emxInit_real_T1(&b_v1, 1);
 5021   
 5022     //  predict angles
 5023     loop_ub = v1->size[0];
 5024     k = b_v1->size[0];
 5025     b_v1->size[0] = loop_ub;
 5026     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)b_v1, k, (int)sizeof(double));
 5027     for (k = 0; k < loop_ub; k++) {
 5028       b_v1->data[k] = v1->data[k + v1->size[0]];
 5029     }
 5030   
 5031     emxInit_real_T1(&c_v1, 1);
 5032     loop_ub = v1->size[0];
 5033     k = c_v1->size[0];
 5034     c_v1->size[0] = loop_ub;
 5035     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)c_v1, k, (int)sizeof(double));
 5036     for (k = 0; k < loop_ub; k++) {
 5037       c_v1->data[k] = v1->data[k];
 5038     }
 5039   
 5040     emxInit_real_T1(&a1, 1);
 5041     emxInit_real_T1(&b_v2, 1);
 5042     c_atan2(b_v1, c_v1, a1);
 5043     loop_ub = v2->size[0];
 5044     k = b_v2->size[0];
 5045     b_v2->size[0] = loop_ub;
 5046     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)b_v2, k, (int)sizeof(double));
 5047     emxFree_real_T(&c_v1);
 5048     emxFree_real_T(&b_v1);
 5049     for (k = 0; k < loop_ub; k++) {
 5050       b_v2->data[k] = v2->data[k + v2->size[0]];
 5051     }
 5052   
 5053     emxInit_real_T1(&c_v2, 1);
 5054     loop_ub = v2->size[0];
 5055     k = c_v2->size[0];
 5056     c_v2->size[0] = loop_ub;
 5057     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)c_v2, k, (int)sizeof(double));
 5058     for (k = 0; k < loop_ub; k++) {
 5059       c_v2->data[k] = v2->data[k];
 5060     }
 5061   
 5062     emxInit_real_T1(&a3, 1);
 5063     c_atan2(b_v2, c_v2, a3);
 5064     k = a3->size[0];
 5065     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)a3, k, (int)sizeof(double));
 5066     loop_ub = a3->size[0];
 5067     emxFree_real_T(&c_v2);
 5068     emxFree_real_T(&b_v2);
 5069     for (k = 0; k < loop_ub; k++) {
 5070       a3->data[k] = 2.0 * a3->data[k] - a1->data[k];
 5071     }
 5072   
 5073     emxInit_real_T1(&d_v1, 1);
 5074   
 5075     //  predict scales
 5076     loop_ub = v1->size[0];
 5077     k = d_v1->size[0];
 5078     d_v1->size[0] = loop_ub;
 5079     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)d_v1, k, (int)sizeof(double));
 5080     for (k = 0; k < loop_ub; k++) {
 5081       d_v1->data[k] = v1->data[k];
 5082     }
 5083   
 5084     emxInit_real_T1(&s1, 1);
 5085     emxInit_real_T1(&e_v1, 1);
 5086     b_power(d_v1, s1);
 5087     loop_ub = v1->size[0];
 5088     k = e_v1->size[0];
 5089     e_v1->size[0] = loop_ub;
 5090     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)e_v1, k, (int)sizeof(double));
 5091     emxFree_real_T(&d_v1);
 5092     for (k = 0; k < loop_ub; k++) {
 5093       e_v1->data[k] = v1->data[k + v1->size[0]];
 5094     }
 5095   
 5096     emxFree_real_T(&v1);
 5097     b_power(e_v1, a1);
 5098     k = s1->size[0];
 5099     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)s1, k, (int)sizeof(double));
 5100     loop_ub = s1->size[0];
 5101     emxFree_real_T(&e_v1);
 5102     for (k = 0; k < loop_ub; k++) {
 5103       s1->data[k] += a1->data[k];
 5104     }
 5105   
 5106     emxInit_real_T1(&d_v2, 1);
 5107     c_sqrt(s1);
 5108     loop_ub = v2->size[0];
 5109     k = d_v2->size[0];
 5110     d_v2->size[0] = loop_ub;
 5111     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)d_v2, k, (int)sizeof(double));
 5112     for (k = 0; k < loop_ub; k++) {
 5113       d_v2->data[k] = v2->data[k];
 5114     }
 5115   
 5116     emxInit_real_T1(&b, 1);
 5117     emxInit_real_T1(&e_v2, 1);
 5118     b_power(d_v2, b);
 5119     loop_ub = v2->size[0];
 5120     k = e_v2->size[0];
 5121     e_v2->size[0] = loop_ub;
 5122     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)e_v2, k, (int)sizeof(double));
 5123     emxFree_real_T(&d_v2);
 5124     for (k = 0; k < loop_ub; k++) {
 5125       e_v2->data[k] = v2->data[k + v2->size[0]];
 5126     }
 5127   
 5128     emxFree_real_T(&v2);
 5129     b_power(e_v2, a1);
 5130     k = b->size[0];
 5131     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)b, k, (int)sizeof(double));
 5132     loop_ub = b->size[0];
 5133     emxFree_real_T(&e_v2);
 5134     for (k = 0; k < loop_ub; k++) {
 5135       b->data[k] += a1->data[k];
 5136     }
 5137   
 5138     c_sqrt(b);
 5139   
 5140     //  predict p3 (the factor 0.75 ensures that under extreme
 5141     //  distortions (omnicam) the closer prediction is selected)
 5142     k = a1->size[0];
 5143     a1->size[0] = a3->size[0];
 5144     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)a1, k, (int)sizeof(double));
 5145     loop_ub = a3->size[0];
 5146     for (k = 0; k < loop_ub; k++) {
 5147       a1->data[k] = a3->data[k];
 5148     }
 5149   
 5150     for (k = 0; k + 1 <= a3->size[0]; k++) {
 5151       a1->data[k] = cos(a1->data[k]);
 5152     }
 5153   
 5154     emxInit_real_T1(&x, 1);
 5155     k = x->size[0];
 5156     x->size[0] = a3->size[0];
 5157     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)x, k, (int)sizeof(double));
 5158     loop_ub = a3->size[0];
 5159     for (k = 0; k < loop_ub; k++) {
 5160       x->data[k] = a3->data[k];
 5161     }
 5162   
 5163     for (k = 0; k + 1 <= a3->size[0]; k++) {
 5164       x->data[k] = sin(x->data[k]);
 5165     }
 5166   
 5167     emxFree_real_T(&a3);
 5168     emxInit_real_T1(&r7, 1);
 5169     k = r7->size[0];
 5170     r7->size[0] = b->size[0];
 5171     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)r7, k, (int)sizeof(double));
 5172     loop_ub = b->size[0];
 5173     for (k = 0; k < loop_ub; k++) {
 5174       r7->data[k] = 0.75 * (2.0 * b->data[k] - s1->data[k]);
 5175     }
 5176   
 5177     emxFree_real_T(&b);
 5178     emxFree_real_T(&s1);
 5179     emxInit_real_T(&r8, 2);
 5180     emxInit_real_T(&b_a1, 2);
 5181     k = r8->size[0] * r8->size[1];
 5182     r8->size[0] = r7->size[0];
 5183     r8->size[1] = 2;
 5184     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)r8, k, (int)sizeof(double));
 5185     loop_ub = r7->size[0];
 5186     for (k = 0; k < loop_ub; k++) {
 5187       for (i12 = 0; i12 < 2; i12++) {
 5188         r8->data[k + r8->size[0] * i12] = r7->data[k];
 5189       }
 5190     }
 5191   
 5192     emxFree_real_T(&r7);
 5193     k = b_a1->size[0] * b_a1->size[1];
 5194     b_a1->size[0] = a1->size[0];
 5195     b_a1->size[1] = 2;
 5196     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)b_a1, k, (int)sizeof(double));
 5197     loop_ub = a1->size[0];
 5198     for (k = 0; k < loop_ub; k++) {
 5199       b_a1->data[k] = a1->data[k];
 5200     }
 5201   
 5202     emxFree_real_T(&a1);
 5203     loop_ub = x->size[0];
 5204     for (k = 0; k < loop_ub; k++) {
 5205       b_a1->data[k + b_a1->size[0]] = x->data[k];
 5206     }
 5207   
 5208     emxFree_real_T(&x);
 5209     k = pred->size[0] * pred->size[1];
 5210     pred->size[0] = p3->size[0];
 5211     pred->size[1] = p3->size[1];
 5212     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)pred, k, (int)sizeof(double));
 5213     loop_ub = p3->size[1];
 5214     for (k = 0; k < loop_ub; k++) {
 5215       b_loop_ub = p3->size[0];
 5216       for (i12 = 0; i12 < b_loop_ub; i12++) {
 5217         pred->data[i12 + pred->size[0] * k] = p3->data[i12 + p3->size[0] * k] +
 5218           r8->data[i12 + r8->size[0] * k] * b_a1->data[i12 + b_a1->size[0] * k];
 5219       }
 5220     }
 5221   
 5222     emxFree_real_T(&b_a1);
 5223     emxFree_real_T(&r8);
 5224   }
 5225   
 5226   //
 5227   // image dimensions
 5228   // Arguments    : const double img_angle[921600]
 5229   //                const double img_weight[921600]
 5230   //                b_struct_T *corners
 5231   //                double r
 5232   // Return Type  : void
 5233   //
 5234   static void refineCorners(const double img_angle[921600], const double
 5235     img_weight[921600], b_struct_T *corners, double r)
 5236   {
 5237     int i;
 5238     emxArray_int32_T *r9;
 5239     emxArray_real_T *b_img_angle;
 5240     emxArray_real_T *b_img_weight;
 5241     double varargin_1;
 5242     double d0;
 5243     int i15;
 5244     int unnamed_idx_1;
 5245     int i16;
 5246     int i17;
 5247     int i18;
 5248     int i19;
 5249     int i20;
 5250     int i21;
 5251     int i22;
 5252     int loop_ub;
 5253     int b_loop_ub;
 5254     double v1[2];
 5255     double v2[2];
 5256   
 5257     //  for all corners do
 5258     i = 0;
 5259     emxInit_int32_T(&r9, 1);
 5260     emxInit_real_T(&b_img_angle, 2);
 5261     emxInit_real_T(&b_img_weight, 2);
 5262     while (i <= corners->p->size[0] - 1) {
 5263       //  extract current corner location
 5264       //  estimate edge orientations
 5265       varargin_1 = corners->p->data[i + corners->p->size[0]] - r;
 5266       if (varargin_1 >= 1.0) {
 5267         d0 = varargin_1;
 5268       } else {
 5269         d0 = 1.0;
 5270       }
 5271   
 5272       varargin_1 = corners->p->data[i + corners->p->size[0]] + r;
 5273       if (varargin_1 <= 720.0) {
 5274       } else {
 5275         varargin_1 = 720.0;
 5276       }
 5277   
 5278       if (d0 > varargin_1) {
 5279         i15 = 0;
 5280         unnamed_idx_1 = 0;
 5281       } else {
 5282         i15 = (int)d0 - 1;
 5283         unnamed_idx_1 = (int)varargin_1;
 5284       }
 5285   
 5286       varargin_1 = corners->p->data[i] - r;
 5287       if (varargin_1 >= 1.0) {
 5288         d0 = varargin_1;
 5289       } else {
 5290         d0 = 1.0;
 5291       }
 5292   
 5293       varargin_1 = corners->p->data[i] + r;
 5294       if (varargin_1 <= 720.0) {
 5295       } else {
 5296         varargin_1 = 720.0;
 5297       }
 5298   
 5299       if (d0 > varargin_1) {
 5300         i16 = 0;
 5301         i17 = 0;
 5302       } else {
 5303         i16 = (int)d0 - 1;
 5304         i17 = (int)varargin_1;
 5305       }
 5306   
 5307       varargin_1 = corners->p->data[i + corners->p->size[0]] - r;
 5308       if (varargin_1 >= 1.0) {
 5309         d0 = varargin_1;
 5310       } else {
 5311         d0 = 1.0;
 5312       }
 5313   
 5314       varargin_1 = corners->p->data[i + corners->p->size[0]] + r;
 5315       if (varargin_1 <= 720.0) {
 5316       } else {
 5317         varargin_1 = 720.0;
 5318       }
 5319   
 5320       if (d0 > varargin_1) {
 5321         i18 = 0;
 5322         i19 = 0;
 5323       } else {
 5324         i18 = (int)d0 - 1;
 5325         i19 = (int)varargin_1;
 5326       }
 5327   
 5328       varargin_1 = corners->p->data[i] - r;
 5329       if (varargin_1 >= 1.0) {
 5330         d0 = varargin_1;
 5331       } else {
 5332         d0 = 1.0;
 5333       }
 5334   
 5335       varargin_1 = corners->p->data[i] + r;
 5336       if (varargin_1 <= 720.0) {
 5337       } else {
 5338         varargin_1 = 720.0;
 5339       }
 5340   
 5341       if (d0 > varargin_1) {
 5342         i20 = 0;
 5343         i21 = 0;
 5344       } else {
 5345         i20 = (int)d0 - 1;
 5346         i21 = (int)varargin_1;
 5347       }
 5348   
 5349       i22 = b_img_angle->size[0] * b_img_angle->size[1];
 5350       b_img_angle->size[0] = unnamed_idx_1 - i15;
 5351       b_img_angle->size[1] = i17 - i16;
 5352       emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)b_img_angle, i22, (int)sizeof(double));
 5353       loop_ub = i17 - i16;
 5354       for (i17 = 0; i17 < loop_ub; i17++) {
 5355         b_loop_ub = unnamed_idx_1 - i15;
 5356         for (i22 = 0; i22 < b_loop_ub; i22++) {
 5357           b_img_angle->data[i22 + b_img_angle->size[0] * i17] = img_angle[(i15 +
 5358             i22) + 720 * (i16 + i17)];
 5359         }
 5360       }
 5361   
 5362       i15 = b_img_weight->size[0] * b_img_weight->size[1];
 5363       b_img_weight->size[0] = i19 - i18;
 5364       b_img_weight->size[1] = i21 - i20;
 5365       emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)b_img_weight, i15, (int)sizeof(double));
 5366       loop_ub = i21 - i20;
 5367       for (i15 = 0; i15 < loop_ub; i15++) {
 5368         b_loop_ub = i19 - i18;
 5369         for (unnamed_idx_1 = 0; unnamed_idx_1 < b_loop_ub; unnamed_idx_1++) {
 5370           b_img_weight->data[unnamed_idx_1 + b_img_weight->size[0] * i15] =
 5371             img_weight[(i18 + unnamed_idx_1) + 720 * (i20 + i15)];
 5372         }
 5373       }
 5374   
 5375       edgeOrientations(b_img_angle, b_img_weight, v1, v2);
 5376       loop_ub = corners->v1->size[1];
 5377       i15 = r9->size[0];
 5378       r9->size[0] = loop_ub;
 5379       emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)r9, i15, (int)sizeof(int));
 5380       for (i15 = 0; i15 < loop_ub; i15++) {
 5381         r9->data[i15] = i15;
 5382       }
 5383   
 5384       unnamed_idx_1 = r9->size[0];
 5385       for (i15 = 0; i15 < unnamed_idx_1; i15++) {
 5386         corners->v1->data[i + corners->v1->size[0] * r9->data[i15]] = v1[i15];
 5387       }
 5388   
 5389       loop_ub = corners->v2->size[1];
 5390       i15 = r9->size[0];
 5391       r9->size[0] = loop_ub;
 5392       emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)r9, i15, (int)sizeof(int));
 5393       for (i15 = 0; i15 < loop_ub; i15++) {
 5394         r9->data[i15] = i15;
 5395       }
 5396   
 5397       unnamed_idx_1 = r9->size[0];
 5398       for (i15 = 0; i15 < unnamed_idx_1; i15++) {
 5399         corners->v2->data[i + corners->v2->size[0] * r9->data[i15]] = v2[i15];
 5400       }
 5401   
 5402       //  continue, if invalid edge orientations
 5403       i++;
 5404     }
 5405   
 5406     emxFree_real_T(&b_img_weight);
 5407     emxFree_real_T(&b_img_angle);
 5408     emxFree_int32_T(&r9);
 5409   }
 5410   
 5411   //
 5412   // Arguments    : double u0
 5413   //                double u1
 5414   // Return Type  : double
 5415   //
 5416   static double rt_atan2d_snf(double u0, double u1)
 5417   {
 5418     double y;
 5419     int b_u0;
 5420     int b_u1;
 5421     if (rtIsNaN(u0) || rtIsNaN(u1)) {
 5422       y = rtNaN;
 5423     } else if (rtIsInf(u0) && rtIsInf(u1)) {
 5424       if (u0 > 0.0) {
 5425         b_u0 = 1;
 5426       } else {
 5427         b_u0 = -1;
 5428       }
 5429   
 5430       if (u1 > 0.0) {
 5431         b_u1 = 1;
 5432       } else {
 5433         b_u1 = -1;
 5434       }
 5435   
 5436       y = atan2((double)b_u0, (double)b_u1);
 5437     } else if (u1 == 0.0) {
 5438       if (u0 > 0.0) {
 5439         y = RT_PI / 2.0;
 5440       } else if (u0 < 0.0) {
 5441         y = -(RT_PI / 2.0);
 5442       } else {
 5443         y = 0.0;
 5444       }
 5445     } else {
 5446       y = atan2(u0, u1);
 5447     }
 5448   
 5449     return y;
 5450   }
 5451   
 5452   //
 5453   // Arguments    : double u
 5454   // Return Type  : double
 5455   //
 5456   static double rt_roundd_snf(double u)
 5457   {
 5458     double y;
 5459     if (fabs(u) < 4.503599627370496E+15) {
 5460       if (u >= 0.5) {
 5461         y = floor(u + 0.5);
 5462       } else if (u > -0.5) {
 5463         y = u * 0.0;
 5464       } else {
 5465         y = ceil(u - 0.5);
 5466       }
 5467     } else {
 5468       y = u;
 5469     }
 5470   
 5471     return y;
 5472   }
 5473   
 5474   //
 5475   // Arguments    : const double img[921600]
 5476   //                const double img_weight[921600]
 5477   //                struct_T *corners
 5478   //                const double radius[3]
 5479   // Return Type  : void
 5480   //
 5481   static void scoreCorners(const double img[921600], const double img_weight
 5482     [921600], struct_T *corners, const double radius[3])
 5483   {
 5484     int i;
 5485     emxArray_real_T *img_sub;
 5486     emxArray_real_T *img_weight_sub;
 5487     emxArray_real_T *v1;
 5488     emxArray_real_T *v2;
 5489     emxArray_real_T *img_filter;
 5490     emxArray_real_T *vec_weight;
 5491     emxArray_real_T *template_a1;
 5492     emxArray_real_T *template_a2;
 5493     emxArray_real_T *template_b1;
 5494     emxArray_real_T *template_b2;
 5495     emxArray_real_T *A;
 5496     emxArray_real_T *b_template_b2;
 5497     emxArray_real_T *b_template_b1;
 5498     emxArray_real_T *b_template_a2;
 5499     emxArray_real_T *b_template_a1;
 5500     emxArray_real_T *b_vec_weight;
 5501     emxArray_real_T *b_v1;
 5502     emxArray_real_T *b_v2;
 5503     double u;
 5504     double v;
 5505     double score[3];
 5506     int j;
 5507     int ixstart;
 5508     double mtmp;
 5509     double varargin_2;
 5510     int ix;
 5511     boolean_T exitg1;
 5512     int i23;
 5513     int i24;
 5514     int i25;
 5515     int i26;
 5516     int i27;
 5517     int i28;
 5518     double c[2];
 5519     int x;
 5520     int y;
 5521     int iv0[1];
 5522     short iv1[2];
 5523     emxArray_real_T b_img_weight_sub;
 5524     double p1[2];
 5525     int iv2[1];
 5526     double b_y;
 5527     int b_img_filter[1];
 5528     double b_p1[2];
 5529     boolean_T guard1 = false;
 5530     int c_img_filter[1];
 5531     double a1;
 5532     double a2;
 5533     double b1;
 5534     double b2;
 5535     double mu;
 5536     double score_a;
 5537     double score_b;
 5538     double score_1;
 5539     double score_2;
 5540     double c_y;
 5541     double b_mtmp;
 5542   
 5543     //  for all corners do
 5544     i = 0;
 5545     emxInit_real_T(&img_sub, 2);
 5546     emxInit_real_T(&img_weight_sub, 2);
 5547     emxInit_real_T(&v1, 2);
 5548     emxInit_real_T(&v2, 2);
 5549     emxInit_real_T(&img_filter, 2);
 5550     emxInit_real_T1(&vec_weight, 1);
 5551     emxInit_real_T(&template_a1, 2);
 5552     emxInit_real_T(&template_a2, 2);
 5553     emxInit_real_T(&template_b1, 2);
 5554     emxInit_real_T(&template_b2, 2);
 5555     emxInit_real_T1(&A, 1);
 5556     emxInit_real_T1(&b_template_b2, 1);
 5557     emxInit_real_T1(&b_template_b1, 1);
 5558     emxInit_real_T1(&b_template_a2, 1);
 5559     emxInit_real_T1(&b_template_a1, 1);
 5560     emxInit_real_T1(&b_vec_weight, 1);
 5561     emxInit_real_T1(&b_v1, 1);
 5562     emxInit_real_T1(&b_v2, 1);
 5563     while (i <= corners->p->size[0] - 1) {
 5564       //  corner location
 5565       u = rt_roundd_snf(corners->p->data[i]);
 5566       v = rt_roundd_snf(corners->p->data[i + corners->p->size[0]]);
 5567   
 5568       //  compute corner statistics @ radius 1
 5569       for (j = 0; j < 3; j++) {
 5570         score[j] = 0.0;
 5571         if ((u > radius[j]) && (u <= 1280.0 - radius[j]) && (v > radius[j]) && (v <=
 5572              720.0 - radius[j])) {
 5573           mtmp = v - radius[j];
 5574           varargin_2 = v + radius[j];
 5575           if (mtmp > varargin_2) {
 5576             i23 = 0;
 5577             i24 = 0;
 5578           } else {
 5579             i23 = (int)mtmp - 1;
 5580             i24 = (int)varargin_2;
 5581           }
 5582   
 5583           mtmp = u - radius[j];
 5584           varargin_2 = u + radius[j];
 5585           if (mtmp > varargin_2) {
 5586             i25 = 0;
 5587             i26 = 0;
 5588           } else {
 5589             i25 = (int)mtmp - 1;
 5590             i26 = (int)varargin_2;
 5591           }
 5592   
 5593           i27 = img_sub->size[0] * img_sub->size[1];
 5594           img_sub->size[0] = i24 - i23;
 5595           img_sub->size[1] = i26 - i25;
 5596           emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)img_sub, i27, (int)sizeof(double));
 5597           ix = i26 - i25;
 5598           for (i26 = 0; i26 < ix; i26++) {
 5599             ixstart = i24 - i23;
 5600             for (i27 = 0; i27 < ixstart; i27++) {
 5601               img_sub->data[i27 + img_sub->size[0] * i26] = img[(i23 + i27) + 720 *
 5602                 (i25 + i26)];
 5603             }
 5604           }
 5605   
 5606           mtmp = v - radius[j];
 5607           varargin_2 = v + radius[j];
 5608           if (mtmp > varargin_2) {
 5609             i23 = 0;
 5610             i24 = 0;
 5611           } else {
 5612             i23 = (int)mtmp - 1;
 5613             i24 = (int)varargin_2;
 5614           }
 5615   
 5616           mtmp = u - radius[j];
 5617           varargin_2 = u + radius[j];
 5618           if (mtmp > varargin_2) {
 5619             i25 = 0;
 5620             i26 = 0;
 5621           } else {
 5622             i25 = (int)mtmp - 1;
 5623             i26 = (int)varargin_2;
 5624           }
 5625   
 5626           i27 = img_weight_sub->size[0] * img_weight_sub->size[1];
 5627           img_weight_sub->size[0] = i24 - i23;
 5628           img_weight_sub->size[1] = i26 - i25;
 5629           emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)img_weight_sub, i27, (int)sizeof
 5630                             (double));
 5631           ix = i26 - i25;
 5632           for (i27 = 0; i27 < ix; i27++) {
 5633             ixstart = i24 - i23;
 5634             for (i28 = 0; i28 < ixstart; i28++) {
 5635               img_weight_sub->data[i28 + img_weight_sub->size[0] * i27] =
 5636                 img_weight[(i23 + i28) + 720 * (i25 + i27)];
 5637             }
 5638           }
 5639   
 5640           ix = corners->v1->size[1];
 5641           i27 = v1->size[0] * v1->size[1];
 5642           v1->size[0] = 1;
 5643           v1->size[1] = ix;
 5644           emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)v1, i27, (int)sizeof(double));
 5645           for (i27 = 0; i27 < ix; i27++) {
 5646             v1->data[v1->size[0] * i27] = corners->v1->data[i + corners->v1->size
 5647               [0] * i27];
 5648           }
 5649   
 5650           ix = corners->v2->size[1];
 5651           i27 = v2->size[0] * v2->size[1];
 5652           v2->size[0] = 1;
 5653           v2->size[1] = ix;
 5654           emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)v2, i27, (int)sizeof(double));
 5655           for (i27 = 0; i27 < ix; i27++) {
 5656             v2->data[v2->size[0] * i27] = corners->v2->data[i + corners->v2->size
 5657               [0] * i27];
 5658           }
 5659   
 5660           //  center
 5661           ixstart = i24 - i23;
 5662           for (i27 = 0; i27 < 2; i27++) {
 5663             c[i27] = ((double)ixstart + 1.0) / 2.0;
 5664           }
 5665   
 5666           //  compute gradient filter kernel (bandwith = 3 px)
 5667           i27 = img_filter->size[0] * img_filter->size[1];
 5668           img_filter->size[0] = i24 - i23;
 5669           img_filter->size[1] = i26 - i25;
 5670           emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)img_filter, i27, (int)sizeof
 5671                             (double));
 5672           ix = (i24 - i23) * (i26 - i25);
 5673           for (i27 = 0; i27 < ix; i27++) {
 5674             img_filter->data[i27] = -1.0;
 5675           }
 5676   
 5677           i27 = (i26 - i25) - 1;
 5678           for (x = 0; x <= i27; x++) {
 5679             i28 = (i24 - i23) - 1;
 5680             for (y = 0; y <= i28; y++) {
 5681               iv1[0] = (short)(1 + x);
 5682               iv1[1] = (short)(1 + y);
 5683               for (ixstart = 0; ixstart < 2; ixstart++) {
 5684                 p1[ixstart] = (double)iv1[ixstart] - c[ixstart];
 5685               }
 5686   
 5687               ixstart = b_v1->size[0];
 5688               b_v1->size[0] = v1->size[1];
 5689               emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)b_v1, ixstart, (int)sizeof
 5690                                 (double));
 5691               ix = v1->size[1];
 5692               for (ixstart = 0; ixstart < ix; ixstart++) {
 5693                 b_v1->data[ixstart] = v1->data[v1->size[0] * ixstart];
 5694               }
 5695   
 5696               b_y = 0.0;
 5697               for (ixstart = 0; ixstart < 2; ixstart++) {
 5698                 b_y += p1[ixstart] * b_v1->data[ixstart];
 5699               }
 5700   
 5701               ixstart = b_v2->size[0];
 5702               b_v2->size[0] = v2->size[1];
 5703               emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)b_v2, ixstart, (int)sizeof
 5704                                 (double));
 5705               ix = v2->size[1];
 5706               for (ixstart = 0; ixstart < ix; ixstart++) {
 5707                 b_v2->data[ixstart] = v2->data[v2->size[0] * ixstart];
 5708               }
 5709   
 5710               mtmp = 0.0;
 5711               for (ixstart = 0; ixstart < 2; ixstart++) {
 5712                 mtmp += p1[ixstart] * b_v2->data[ixstart];
 5713               }
 5714   
 5715               for (ixstart = 0; ixstart < 2; ixstart++) {
 5716                 b_p1[ixstart] = p1[ixstart] - b_y * v1->data[ixstart];
 5717               }
 5718   
 5719               guard1 = false;
 5720               if (norm(b_p1) <= 1.5) {
 5721                 guard1 = true;
 5722               } else {
 5723                 for (ixstart = 0; ixstart < 2; ixstart++) {
 5724                   b_p1[ixstart] = p1[ixstart] - mtmp * v2->data[ixstart];
 5725                 }
 5726   
 5727                 if (norm(b_p1) <= 1.5) {
 5728                   guard1 = true;
 5729                 }
 5730               }
 5731   
 5732               if (guard1) {
 5733                 img_filter->data[y + img_filter->size[0] * x] = 1.0;
 5734               }
 5735             }
 5736           }
 5737   
 5738           //  convert into vectors
 5739           //  normalize
 5740           ixstart = i24 - i23;
 5741           ix = i26 - i25;
 5742           iv0[0] = (i24 - i23) * (i26 - i25);
 5743           b_img_weight_sub = *img_weight_sub;
 5744           b_img_weight_sub.size = (int *)&iv0;
 5745           b_img_weight_sub.numDimensions = 1;
 5746           mtmp = mean(&b_img_weight_sub);
 5747           i27 = vec_weight->size[0];
 5748           vec_weight->size[0] = ixstart * ix;
 5749           emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)vec_weight, i27, (int)sizeof
 5750                             (double));
 5751           ix *= ixstart;
 5752           for (i27 = 0; i27 < ix; i27++) {
 5753             vec_weight->data[i27] = img_weight_sub->data[i27] - mtmp;
 5754           }
 5755   
 5756           iv2[0] = (i24 - i23) * (i26 - i25);
 5757           b_img_weight_sub = *img_weight_sub;
 5758           b_img_weight_sub.size = (int *)&iv2;
 5759           b_img_weight_sub.numDimensions = 1;
 5760           b_y = b_std(&b_img_weight_sub);
 5761           i23 = vec_weight->size[0];
 5762           emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)vec_weight, i23, (int)sizeof
 5763                             (double));
 5764           ix = vec_weight->size[0];
 5765           for (i23 = 0; i23 < ix; i23++) {
 5766             vec_weight->data[i23] /= b_y;
 5767           }
 5768   
 5769           b_img_filter[0] = img_filter->size[0] * img_filter->size[1];
 5770           b_img_weight_sub = *img_filter;
 5771           b_img_weight_sub.size = (int *)&b_img_filter;
 5772           b_img_weight_sub.numDimensions = 1;
 5773           mtmp = mean(&b_img_weight_sub);
 5774           i23 = A->size[0];
 5775           A->size[0] = img_filter->size[0] * img_filter->size[1];
 5776           emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)A, i23, (int)sizeof(double));
 5777           ix = img_filter->size[0] * img_filter->size[1];
 5778           for (i23 = 0; i23 < ix; i23++) {
 5779             A->data[i23] = img_filter->data[i23] - mtmp;
 5780           }
 5781   
 5782           c_img_filter[0] = img_filter->size[0] * img_filter->size[1];
 5783           b_img_weight_sub = *img_filter;
 5784           b_img_weight_sub.size = (int *)&c_img_filter;
 5785           b_img_weight_sub.numDimensions = 1;
 5786           b_y = b_std(&b_img_weight_sub);
 5787   
 5788           //  compute gradient score
 5789           i23 = b_vec_weight->size[0];
 5790           b_vec_weight->size[0] = vec_weight->size[0];
 5791           emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)b_vec_weight, i23, (int)sizeof
 5792                             (double));
 5793           ix = vec_weight->size[0];
 5794           for (i23 = 0; i23 < ix; i23++) {
 5795             b_vec_weight->data[i23] = vec_weight->data[i23] * (A->data[i23] / b_y);
 5796           }
 5797   
 5798           mtmp = sum(b_vec_weight);
 5799           b_y = mtmp / ((double)vec_weight->size[0] - 1.0);
 5800   
 5801           //  create intensity filter kernel
 5802           createCorrelationPatch(rt_atan2d_snf(corners->v1->data[i + corners->
 5803             v1->size[0]], corners->v1->data[i]), rt_atan2d_snf(corners->v2->data[i
 5804             + corners->v2->size[0]], corners->v2->data[i]), c[0] - 1.0,
 5805             template_a1, template_a2, template_b1, template_b2);
 5806   
 5807           //  checkerboard responses
 5808           i23 = b_template_a1->size[0];
 5809           b_template_a1->size[0] = template_a1->size[0] * template_a1->size[1];
 5810           emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)b_template_a1, i23, (int)sizeof
 5811                             (double));
 5812           ix = template_a1->size[0] * template_a1->size[1];
 5813           for (i23 = 0; i23 < ix; i23++) {
 5814             b_template_a1->data[i23] = template_a1->data[i23] * img_sub->data[i23];
 5815           }
 5816   
 5817           a1 = sum(b_template_a1);
 5818           i23 = b_template_a2->size[0];
 5819           b_template_a2->size[0] = template_a2->size[0] * template_a2->size[1];
 5820           emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)b_template_a2, i23, (int)sizeof
 5821                             (double));
 5822           ix = template_a2->size[0] * template_a2->size[1];
 5823           for (i23 = 0; i23 < ix; i23++) {
 5824             b_template_a2->data[i23] = template_a2->data[i23] * img_sub->data[i23];
 5825           }
 5826   
 5827           a2 = sum(b_template_a2);
 5828           i23 = b_template_b1->size[0];
 5829           b_template_b1->size[0] = template_b1->size[0] * template_b1->size[1];
 5830           emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)b_template_b1, i23, (int)sizeof
 5831                             (double));
 5832           ix = template_b1->size[0] * template_b1->size[1];
 5833           for (i23 = 0; i23 < ix; i23++) {
 5834             b_template_b1->data[i23] = template_b1->data[i23] * img_sub->data[i23];
 5835           }
 5836   
 5837           b1 = sum(b_template_b1);
 5838           i23 = b_template_b2->size[0];
 5839           b_template_b2->size[0] = template_b2->size[0] * template_b2->size[1];
 5840           emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)b_template_b2, i23, (int)sizeof
 5841                             (double));
 5842           ix = template_b2->size[0] * template_b2->size[1];
 5843           for (i23 = 0; i23 < ix; i23++) {
 5844             b_template_b2->data[i23] = template_b2->data[i23] * img_sub->data[i23];
 5845           }
 5846   
 5847           b2 = sum(b_template_b2);
 5848   
 5849           //  mean
 5850           mu = (((a1 + a2) + b1) + b2) / 4.0;
 5851   
 5852           //  case 1: a=white, b=black
 5853           mtmp = a1 - mu;
 5854           varargin_2 = a2 - mu;
 5855           if ((mtmp <= varargin_2) || rtIsNaN(varargin_2)) {
 5856             score_a = mtmp;
 5857           } else {
 5858             score_a = varargin_2;
 5859           }
 5860   
 5861           mtmp = mu - b1;
 5862           varargin_2 = mu - b2;
 5863           if ((mtmp <= varargin_2) || rtIsNaN(varargin_2)) {
 5864             score_b = mtmp;
 5865           } else {
 5866             score_b = varargin_2;
 5867           }
 5868   
 5869           if ((score_a <= score_b) || rtIsNaN(score_b)) {
 5870             score_1 = score_a;
 5871           } else {
 5872             score_1 = score_b;
 5873           }
 5874   
 5875           //  case 2: b=white, a=black
 5876           mtmp = mu - a1;
 5877           varargin_2 = mu - a2;
 5878           if ((mtmp <= varargin_2) || rtIsNaN(varargin_2)) {
 5879             score_a = mtmp;
 5880           } else {
 5881             score_a = varargin_2;
 5882           }
 5883   
 5884           mtmp = b1 - mu;
 5885           varargin_2 = b2 - mu;
 5886           if ((mtmp <= varargin_2) || rtIsNaN(varargin_2)) {
 5887             score_b = mtmp;
 5888           } else {
 5889             score_b = varargin_2;
 5890           }
 5891   
 5892           if ((score_a <= score_b) || rtIsNaN(score_b)) {
 5893             score_2 = score_a;
 5894           } else {
 5895             score_2 = score_b;
 5896           }
 5897   
 5898           //  intensity score: max. of the 2 cases
 5899           if ((score_1 >= score_2) || rtIsNaN(score_2)) {
 5900             mtmp = score_1;
 5901           } else {
 5902             mtmp = score_2;
 5903           }
 5904   
 5905           //  final score: product of gradient and intensity score
 5906           if (b_y >= 0.0) {
 5907             c_y = b_y;
 5908           } else {
 5909             c_y = 0.0;
 5910           }
 5911   
 5912           if (mtmp >= 0.0) {
 5913             b_mtmp = mtmp;
 5914           } else {
 5915             b_mtmp = 0.0;
 5916           }
 5917   
 5918           score[j] = c_y * b_mtmp;
 5919         }
 5920       }
 5921   
 5922       //  take highest score
 5923       ixstart = 1;
 5924       mtmp = score[0];
 5925       if (rtIsNaN(score[0])) {
 5926         ix = 2;
 5927         exitg1 = false;
 5928         while ((!exitg1) && (ix < 4)) {
 5929           ixstart = ix;
 5930           if (!rtIsNaN(score[ix - 1])) {
 5931             mtmp = score[ix - 1];
 5932             exitg1 = true;
 5933           } else {
 5934             ix++;
 5935           }
 5936         }
 5937       }
 5938   
 5939       if (ixstart < 3) {
 5940         while (ixstart + 1 < 4) {
 5941           if (score[ixstart] > mtmp) {
 5942             mtmp = score[ixstart];
 5943           }
 5944   
 5945           ixstart++;
 5946         }
 5947       }
 5948   
 5949       corners->score->data[i] = mtmp;
 5950       i++;
 5951     }
 5952   
 5953     emxFree_real_T(&b_v2);
 5954     emxFree_real_T(&b_v1);
 5955     emxFree_real_T(&b_vec_weight);
 5956     emxFree_real_T(&b_template_a1);
 5957     emxFree_real_T(&b_template_a2);
 5958     emxFree_real_T(&b_template_b1);
 5959     emxFree_real_T(&b_template_b2);
 5960     emxFree_real_T(&A);
 5961     emxFree_real_T(&template_b2);
 5962     emxFree_real_T(&template_b1);
 5963     emxFree_real_T(&template_a2);
 5964     emxFree_real_T(&template_a1);
 5965     emxFree_real_T(&vec_weight);
 5966     emxFree_real_T(&img_filter);
 5967     emxFree_real_T(&v2);
 5968     emxFree_real_T(&v1);
 5969     emxFree_real_T(&img_weight_sub);
 5970     emxFree_real_T(&img_sub);
 5971   }
 5972   
 5973   //
 5974   // Arguments    : emxArray_real_T *x
 5975   //                emxArray_int32_T *idx
 5976   // Return Type  : void
 5977   //
 5978   static void sort(emxArray_real_T *x, emxArray_int32_T *idx)
 5979   {
 5980     emxArray_real_T *b_x;
 5981     unsigned int unnamed_idx_0;
 5982     int ib;
 5983     int m;
 5984     int n;
 5985     double x4[4];
 5986     int idx4[4];
 5987     emxArray_int32_T *iwork;
 5988     emxArray_real_T *xwork;
 5989     int nNaNs;
 5990     int k;
 5991     int wOffset;
 5992     signed char perm[4];
 5993     int nNonNaN;
 5994     int p;
 5995     int i4;
 5996     int nBlocks;
 5997     int b_iwork[256];
 5998     double b_xwork[256];
 5999     int b;
 6000     int bLen;
 6001     int bLen2;
 6002     int nPairs;
 6003     int exitg1;
 6004     emxInit_real_T1(&b_x, 1);
 6005     unnamed_idx_0 = (unsigned int)x->size[0];
 6006     ib = b_x->size[0];
 6007     b_x->size[0] = x->size[0];
 6008     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)b_x, ib, (int)sizeof(double));
 6009     m = x->size[0];
 6010     for (ib = 0; ib < m; ib++) {
 6011       b_x->data[ib] = x->data[ib];
 6012     }
 6013   
 6014     ib = idx->size[0];
 6015     idx->size[0] = (int)unnamed_idx_0;
 6016     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)idx, ib, (int)sizeof(int));
 6017     m = (int)unnamed_idx_0;
 6018     for (ib = 0; ib < m; ib++) {
 6019       idx->data[ib] = 0;
 6020     }
 6021   
 6022     n = x->size[0];
 6023     for (m = 0; m < 4; m++) {
 6024       x4[m] = 0.0;
 6025       idx4[m] = 0;
 6026     }
 6027   
 6028     emxInit_int32_T(&iwork, 1);
 6029     ib = iwork->size[0];
 6030     iwork->size[0] = (int)unnamed_idx_0;
 6031     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)iwork, ib, (int)sizeof(int));
 6032     m = iwork->size[0];
 6033     ib = iwork->size[0];
 6034     iwork->size[0] = m;
 6035     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)iwork, ib, (int)sizeof(int));
 6036     for (ib = 0; ib < m; ib++) {
 6037       iwork->data[ib] = 0;
 6038     }
 6039   
 6040     emxInit_real_T1(&xwork, 1);
 6041     unnamed_idx_0 = (unsigned int)x->size[0];
 6042     ib = xwork->size[0];
 6043     xwork->size[0] = (int)unnamed_idx_0;
 6044     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)xwork, ib, (int)sizeof(double));
 6045     m = xwork->size[0];
 6046     ib = xwork->size[0];
 6047     xwork->size[0] = m;
 6048     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)xwork, ib, (int)sizeof(double));
 6049     for (ib = 0; ib < m; ib++) {
 6050       xwork->data[ib] = 0.0;
 6051     }
 6052   
 6053     nNaNs = 0;
 6054     ib = 0;
 6055     for (k = 0; k + 1 <= n; k++) {
 6056       if (rtIsNaN(b_x->data[k])) {
 6057         idx->data[(n - nNaNs) - 1] = k + 1;
 6058         xwork->data[(n - nNaNs) - 1] = b_x->data[k];
 6059         nNaNs++;
 6060       } else {
 6061         ib++;
 6062         idx4[ib - 1] = k + 1;
 6063         x4[ib - 1] = b_x->data[k];
 6064         if (ib == 4) {
 6065           ib = k - nNaNs;
 6066           if (x4[0] >= x4[1]) {
 6067             m = 1;
 6068             wOffset = 2;
 6069           } else {
 6070             m = 2;
 6071             wOffset = 1;
 6072           }
 6073   
 6074           if (x4[2] >= x4[3]) {
 6075             p = 3;
 6076             i4 = 4;
 6077           } else {
 6078             p = 4;
 6079             i4 = 3;
 6080           }
 6081   
 6082           if (x4[m - 1] >= x4[p - 1]) {
 6083             if (x4[wOffset - 1] >= x4[p - 1]) {
 6084               perm[0] = (signed char)m;
 6085               perm[1] = (signed char)wOffset;
 6086               perm[2] = (signed char)p;
 6087               perm[3] = (signed char)i4;
 6088             } else if (x4[wOffset - 1] >= x4[i4 - 1]) {
 6089               perm[0] = (signed char)m;
 6090               perm[1] = (signed char)p;
 6091               perm[2] = (signed char)wOffset;
 6092               perm[3] = (signed char)i4;
 6093             } else {
 6094               perm[0] = (signed char)m;
 6095               perm[1] = (signed char)p;
 6096               perm[2] = (signed char)i4;
 6097               perm[3] = (signed char)wOffset;
 6098             }
 6099           } else if (x4[m - 1] >= x4[i4 - 1]) {
 6100             if (x4[wOffset - 1] >= x4[i4 - 1]) {
 6101               perm[0] = (signed char)p;
 6102               perm[1] = (signed char)m;
 6103               perm[2] = (signed char)wOffset;
 6104               perm[3] = (signed char)i4;
 6105             } else {
 6106               perm[0] = (signed char)p;
 6107               perm[1] = (signed char)m;
 6108               perm[2] = (signed char)i4;
 6109               perm[3] = (signed char)wOffset;
 6110             }
 6111           } else {
 6112             perm[0] = (signed char)p;
 6113             perm[1] = (signed char)i4;
 6114             perm[2] = (signed char)m;
 6115             perm[3] = (signed char)wOffset;
 6116           }
 6117   
 6118           idx->data[ib - 3] = idx4[perm[0] - 1];
 6119           idx->data[ib - 2] = idx4[perm[1] - 1];
 6120           idx->data[ib - 1] = idx4[perm[2] - 1];
 6121           idx->data[ib] = idx4[perm[3] - 1];
 6122           b_x->data[ib - 3] = x4[perm[0] - 1];
 6123           b_x->data[ib - 2] = x4[perm[1] - 1];
 6124           b_x->data[ib - 1] = x4[perm[2] - 1];
 6125           b_x->data[ib] = x4[perm[3] - 1];
 6126           ib = 0;
 6127         }
 6128       }
 6129     }
 6130   
 6131     wOffset = (x->size[0] - nNaNs) - 1;
 6132     if (ib > 0) {
 6133       for (m = 0; m < 4; m++) {
 6134         perm[m] = 0;
 6135       }
 6136   
 6137       if (ib == 1) {
 6138         perm[0] = 1;
 6139       } else if (ib == 2) {
 6140         if (x4[0] >= x4[1]) {
 6141           perm[0] = 1;
 6142           perm[1] = 2;
 6143         } else {
 6144           perm[0] = 2;
 6145           perm[1] = 1;
 6146         }
 6147       } else if (x4[0] >= x4[1]) {
 6148         if (x4[1] >= x4[2]) {
 6149           perm[0] = 1;
 6150           perm[1] = 2;
 6151           perm[2] = 3;
 6152         } else if (x4[0] >= x4[2]) {
 6153           perm[0] = 1;
 6154           perm[1] = 3;
 6155           perm[2] = 2;
 6156         } else {
 6157           perm[0] = 3;
 6158           perm[1] = 1;
 6159           perm[2] = 2;
 6160         }
 6161       } else if (x4[0] >= x4[2]) {
 6162         perm[0] = 2;
 6163         perm[1] = 1;
 6164         perm[2] = 3;
 6165       } else if (x4[1] >= x4[2]) {
 6166         perm[0] = 2;
 6167         perm[1] = 3;
 6168         perm[2] = 1;
 6169       } else {
 6170         perm[0] = 3;
 6171         perm[1] = 2;
 6172         perm[2] = 1;
 6173       }
 6174   
 6175       for (k = 1; k <= ib; k++) {
 6176         idx->data[(wOffset - ib) + k] = idx4[perm[k - 1] - 1];
 6177         b_x->data[(wOffset - ib) + k] = x4[perm[k - 1] - 1];
 6178       }
 6179     }
 6180   
 6181     m = nNaNs >> 1;
 6182     for (k = 1; k <= m; k++) {
 6183       ib = idx->data[wOffset + k];
 6184       idx->data[wOffset + k] = idx->data[n - k];
 6185       idx->data[n - k] = ib;
 6186       b_x->data[wOffset + k] = xwork->data[n - k];
 6187       b_x->data[n - k] = xwork->data[wOffset + k];
 6188     }
 6189   
 6190     if ((nNaNs & 1) != 0) {
 6191       b_x->data[(wOffset + m) + 1] = xwork->data[(wOffset + m) + 1];
 6192     }
 6193   
 6194     nNonNaN = x->size[0] - nNaNs;
 6195     m = 2;
 6196     if (nNonNaN > 1) {
 6197       if (x->size[0] >= 256) {
 6198         nBlocks = nNonNaN >> 8;
 6199         if (nBlocks > 0) {
 6200           for (i4 = 1; i4 <= nBlocks; i4++) {
 6201             n = (i4 - 1) << 8;
 6202             for (b = 0; b < 6; b++) {
 6203               bLen = 1 << (b + 2);
 6204               bLen2 = bLen << 1;
 6205               nPairs = 256 >> (b + 3);
 6206               for (k = 1; k <= nPairs; k++) {
 6207                 m = n + (k - 1) * bLen2;
 6208                 for (ib = 0; ib + 1 <= bLen2; ib++) {
 6209                   b_iwork[ib] = idx->data[m + ib];
 6210                   b_xwork[ib] = b_x->data[m + ib];
 6211                 }
 6212   
 6213                 p = 0;
 6214                 wOffset = bLen;
 6215                 ib = m - 1;
 6216                 do {
 6217                   exitg1 = 0;
 6218                   ib++;
 6219                   if (b_xwork[p] >= b_xwork[wOffset]) {
 6220                     idx->data[ib] = b_iwork[p];
 6221                     b_x->data[ib] = b_xwork[p];
 6222                     if (p + 1 < bLen) {
 6223                       p++;
 6224                     } else {
 6225                       exitg1 = 1;
 6226                     }
 6227                   } else {
 6228                     idx->data[ib] = b_iwork[wOffset];
 6229                     b_x->data[ib] = b_xwork[wOffset];
 6230                     if (wOffset + 1 < bLen2) {
 6231                       wOffset++;
 6232                     } else {
 6233                       ib = (ib - p) + 1;
 6234                       while (p + 1 <= bLen) {
 6235                         idx->data[ib + p] = b_iwork[p];
 6236                         b_x->data[ib + p] = b_xwork[p];
 6237                         p++;
 6238                       }
 6239   
 6240                       exitg1 = 1;
 6241                     }
 6242                   }
 6243                 } while (exitg1 == 0);
 6244               }
 6245             }
 6246           }
 6247   
 6248           m = nBlocks << 8;
 6249           ib = nNonNaN - m;
 6250           if (ib > 0) {
 6251             merge_block(idx, b_x, m, ib, 2, iwork, xwork);
 6252           }
 6253   
 6254           m = 8;
 6255         }
 6256       }
 6257   
 6258       merge_block(idx, b_x, 0, nNonNaN, m, iwork, xwork);
 6259     }
 6260   
 6261     if ((nNaNs > 0) && (nNonNaN > 0)) {
 6262       for (k = 0; k + 1 <= nNaNs; k++) {
 6263         xwork->data[k] = b_x->data[nNonNaN + k];
 6264         iwork->data[k] = idx->data[nNonNaN + k];
 6265       }
 6266   
 6267       for (k = nNonNaN - 1; k + 1 > 0; k--) {
 6268         b_x->data[nNaNs + k] = b_x->data[k];
 6269         idx->data[nNaNs + k] = idx->data[k];
 6270       }
 6271   
 6272       for (k = 0; k + 1 <= nNaNs; k++) {
 6273         b_x->data[k] = xwork->data[k];
 6274         idx->data[k] = iwork->data[k];
 6275       }
 6276     }
 6277   
 6278     emxFree_real_T(&xwork);
 6279     emxFree_int32_T(&iwork);
 6280     ib = x->size[0];
 6281     x->size[0] = b_x->size[0];
 6282     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)x, ib, (int)sizeof(double));
 6283     m = b_x->size[0];
 6284     for (ib = 0; ib < m; ib++) {
 6285       x->data[ib] = b_x->data[ib];
 6286     }
 6287   
 6288     emxFree_real_T(&b_x);
 6289   }
 6290   
 6291   //
 6292   // Arguments    : const emxArray_real_T *x
 6293   // Return Type  : double
 6294   //
 6295   static double sum(const emxArray_real_T *x)
 6296   {
 6297     double y;
 6298     int k;
 6299     if (x->size[0] == 0) {
 6300       y = 0.0;
 6301     } else {
 6302       y = x->data[0];
 6303       for (k = 2; k <= x->size[0]; k++) {
 6304         y += x->data[k - 1];
 6305       }
 6306     }
 6307   
 6308     return y;
 6309   }

 6311   //
 6312   // Arguments    : int numDimensions
 6313   //                int *size
 6314   // Return Type  : emxArray_real_T *
 6315   //
 6316   emxArray_real_T *emxCreateND_real_T(int numDimensions, int *size)
 6317   {
 6318     emxArray_real_T *emx;
 6319     int numEl;
 6320     int i;
 6321     emxInit_real_T(&emx, numDimensions);
 6322     numEl = 1;
 6323     for (i = 0; i < numDimensions; i++) {
 6324       numEl *= size[i];
 6325       emx->size[i] = size[i];
 6326     }
 6327   
 6328     emx->data = (double *)calloc((unsigned int)numEl, sizeof(double));
 6329     emx->numDimensions = numDimensions;
 6330     emx->allocatedSize = numEl;
 6331     return emx;
 6332   }

 6338   // Return Type  : emxArray_real_T *
 6339   //
 6340   emxArray_real_T *emxCreateWrapperND_real_T(double *data, int numDimensions, int *
 6341     size)
 6342   {
 6343     emxArray_real_T *emx;
 6344     int numEl;
 6345     int i;
 6346     emxInit_real_T(&emx, numDimensions);
 6347     numEl = 1;
 6348     for (i = 0; i < numDimensions; i++) {
 6349       numEl *= size[i];
 6350       emx->size[i] = size[i];
 6351     }
 6352   
 6353     emx->data = data;
 6354     emx->numDimensions = numDimensions;
 6355     emx->allocatedSize = numEl;
 6356     emx->canFreeData = false;
 6357     return emx;
 6358   }

 6360   //
 6361   // Arguments    : double *data
 6362   //                int rows
 6363   //                int cols
 6364   // Return Type  : emxArray_real_T *
 6365   //
 6366   emxArray_real_T *emxCreateWrapper_real_T(double *data, int rows, int cols)
 6367   {
 6368     emxArray_real_T *emx;
 6369     int size[2];
 6370     int numEl;
 6371     int i;
 6372     size[0] = rows;
 6373     size[1] = cols;
 6374     emxInit_real_T(&emx, 2);
 6375     numEl = 1;
 6376     for (i = 0; i < 2; i++) {
 6377       numEl *= size[i];
 6378       emx->size[i] = size[i];
 6379     }
 6380   
 6381     emx->data = data;
 6382     emx->numDimensions = 2;
 6383     emx->allocatedSize = numEl;
 6384     emx->canFreeData = false;
 6385     return emx;
 6386   }

 6389   // Arguments    : int rows
 6390   //                int cols
 6391   // Return Type  : emxArray_real_T *
 6392   //
 6393   emxArray_real_T *emxCreate_real_T(int rows, int cols)
 6394   {
 6395     emxArray_real_T *emx;
 6396     int size[2];
 6397     int numEl;
 6398     int i;
 6399     size[0] = rows;
 6400     size[1] = cols;
 6401     emxInit_real_T(&emx, 2);
 6402     numEl = 1;
 6403     for (i = 0; i < 2; i++) {
 6404       numEl *= size[i];
 6405       emx->size[i] = size[i];
 6406     }
 6407   
 6408     emx->data = (double *)calloc((unsigned int)numEl, sizeof(double));
 6409     emx->numDimensions = 2;
 6410     emx->allocatedSize = numEl;
 6411     return emx;
 6412   }

 6434   // Arguments    : const unsigned char image[921600]
 6435   //                emxArray_real_T *corners_uv
 6436   //                emxArray_real_T *tam_chess

 6439   void fce(const unsigned char image[921600], emxArray_real_T *corners_uv,
 6440            emxArray_real_T *tam_chess)
 6441   {

 6454     int exitg2;
 6455     int nrowx;
 6456     int j;
 6457     emxArray_real_T *c_corners_uv;
 6458     unsigned int b_chessboards[2];
 6459     int i0;
 6460     emxArray_boolean_T *b_y;
 6461     int i2;
 6462     emxArray_boolean_T *c_y;
 6463     boolean_T exitg1;
 6464     emxInit_real_T(&corners_p, 2);
 6465     emxInitStruct_struct_T(&expl_temp);
 6466     findCorners(image, 0.01, &expl_temp);
 6467     ix = corners_p->size[0] * corners_p->size[1];
 6468     corners_p->size[0] = expl_temp.p->size[0];
 6469     corners_p->size[1] = expl_temp.p->size[1];
 6470     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)corners_p, ix, (int)sizeof(double));
 6471     ncolx = expl_temp.p->size[0] * expl_temp.p->size[1];
 6472     for (ix = 0; ix < ncolx; ix++) {
 6473       corners_p->data[ix] = expl_temp.p->data[ix];
 6474     }
 6475   
 6476     emxInit_real_T(&corners_v1, 2);
 6477     ix = corners_v1->size[0] * corners_v1->size[1];
 6478     corners_v1->size[0] = expl_temp.v1->size[0];
 6479     corners_v1->size[1] = expl_temp.v1->size[1];
 6480     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)corners_v1, ix, (int)sizeof(double));
 6481     ncolx = expl_temp.v1->size[0] * expl_temp.v1->size[1];
 6482     for (ix = 0; ix < ncolx; ix++) {
 6483       corners_v1->data[ix] = expl_temp.v1->data[ix];
 6484     }
 6485

 6487     ix = corners_v2->size[0] * corners_v2->size[1];
 6488     corners_v2->size[0] = expl_temp.v2->size[0];

 6493       corners_v2->data[ix] = expl_temp.v2->data[ix];
 6494     }

 6497     emxInitMatrix_cell_wrap_0(chessboards);
 6498     chessboardsFromCorners(corners_p, corners_v1, corners_v2, chessboards);
 6499   
 6500     // figure; imshow(uint8(image)); hold on;
 6501     // plotChessboards(chessboards,corners);
 6502     ix = corners_uv->size[0] * corners_uv->size[1];
 6503     corners_uv->size[0] = 1;
