 6506     emxFree_real_T(&corners_v2);
 6507     emxFree_real_T(&corners_v1);
 6508     for (ix = 0; ix < 2; ix++) {
 6509       corners_uv->data[ix] = 0.0;
 6510     }
 6511   
 6512     ix = tam_chess->size[0] * tam_chess->size[1];
 6513     tam_chess->size[0] = 5;
 6514     tam_chess->size[1] = 2;
 6515     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)tam_chess, ix, (int)sizeof(double));
 6516     for (ix = 0; ix < 10; ix++) {
 6517       tam_chess->data[ix] = 0.0;
 6518     }
 6519   
 6520     emxInit_real_T(&p, 2);
 6521     emxInit_int32_T(&r0, 1);
 6522     emxInit_real_T(&b_corners_uv, 2);
 6523     for (i = 0; i < 5; i++) {
 6524       y = true;
 6525       ix = 1;
 6526       do {
 6527         exitg2 = 0;
 6528         nrowx = chessboards[i].f1->size[0] * chessboards[i].f1->size[1];
 6529         if (ix <= nrowx) {
 6530           if (chessboards[i].f1->data[ix - 1] == 0.0) {
 6531             y = false;
 6532             exitg2 = 1;
 6533           } else {
 6534             ix++;
 6535           }
 6536         } else {
 6537           exitg2 = 1;
 6538         }
 6539       } while (exitg2 == 0);
 6540   
 6541       if (y) {
 6542         ix = r0->size[0];
 6543         r0->size[0] = 2;
 6544         emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)r0, ix, (int)sizeof(int));
 6545         for (ix = 0; ix < 2; ix++) {
 6546           r0->data[ix] = ix;
 6547         }
 6548   
 6549         b_chessboards[0] = (unsigned int)chessboards[i].f1->size[0];
 6550         b_chessboards[1] = (unsigned int)chessboards[i].f1->size[1];
 6551         for (ix = 0; ix < 2; ix++) {
 6552           tam_chess->data[i + tam_chess->size[0] * r0->data[ix]] =
 6553             b_chessboards[ix];
 6554         }
 6555   
 6556         for (j = 0; j < chessboards[i].f1->size[0]; j++) {
 6557           ncolx = chessboards[i].f1->size[1];
 6558           nrowx = corners_p->size[1];
 6559           ix = p->size[0] * p->size[1];
 6560           p->size[0] = ncolx;
 6561           p->size[1] = nrowx;
 6562           emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)p, ix, (int)sizeof(double));
 6563           for (ix = 0; ix < nrowx; ix++) {
 6564             for (i0 = 0; i0 < ncolx; i0++) {
 6565               p->data[i0 + p->size[0] * ix] = corners_p->data[((int)chessboards[i]
 6566                 .f1->data[j + chessboards[i].f1->size[0] * i0] + corners_p->size[0]
 6567                 * ix) - 1] + 1.0;
 6568             }
 6569           }
 6570   
 6571           if (!(corners_uv->size[0] == 0)) {
 6572             nrowx = corners_uv->size[1];
 6573           } else if (!((p->size[0] == 0) || (p->size[1] == 0))) {
 6574             nrowx = p->size[1];
 6575           } else {
 6576             nrowx = corners_uv->size[1];
 6577             if (p->size[1] > nrowx) {
 6578               nrowx = p->size[1];
 6579             }
 6580           }
 6581   
 6582           if (!(corners_uv->size[0] == 0)) {
 6583             ncolx = corners_uv->size[0];
 6584           } else {

 6586           }

 6588           if (!((p->size[0] == 0) || (p->size[1] == 0))) {
 6589             i2 = p->size[0];
 6590           } else {

 6592           }
 6593   
 6594           ix = b_corners_uv->size[0] * b_corners_uv->size[1];
 6595           b_corners_uv->size[0] = ncolx + i2;

 6598                             (double));

 6612   
 6613           ix = corners_uv->size[0] * corners_uv->size[1];
 6614           corners_uv->size[0] = b_corners_uv->size[0];
 6615           corners_uv->size[1] = b_corners_uv->size[1];
 6616           emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)corners_uv, ix, (int)sizeof(double));
 6617           ncolx = b_corners_uv->size[1];
 6618           for (ix = 0; ix < ncolx; ix++) {
 6619             nrowx = b_corners_uv->size[0];
 6620             for (i0 = 0; i0 < nrowx; i0++) {

 6639           corners_uv->size[0] * j];

 6661

 6709     for (ix = 0; ix < ncolx; ix++) {
 6710       c_y->data[ix] = !b_y->data[ix];
 6711     }
 6712   
 6713     emxFree_boolean_T(&b_y);
 6714     nullAssignment(tam_chess, c_y);
 6715     emxFree_boolean_T(&c_y);
